href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　任兖州司法参军。受苏轼、范纯仁、丰稷、曾肇等的举荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　同黄庭坚定交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　有画见于苏轼、黄庭坚、晁补之题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　与刘斯立、李资道唱和。作品：《对月偶成》《还资道、斯立诗卷》《和斯立见和诗卷》《和资道读王绩传》《和资道读贺知章传》《送斯立入京》《资道俾予赋试剑山诗马上承命作》《和资道故山驿早行》《和资道山路见菊杂言》《和资道岩岩亭二首》《和资道夜校试卷呈同舍十二韵》《再和资道》《再和》《和斯立重赋》《和资道登岱顶回》<div id='poem_197364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>对月偶成<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197364")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197364_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_197364_0'>① 元祐丁卯，年二十四（按晁说之生于仁宗嘉祐四年[一○五九]，元祐二年丁卯[一○八七]当为二十九岁，此作年二十四，误），为兖州法掾，考试历城，与刘跂斯立、李深资道唱和，凡二十六首，内六首见律诗卷。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197364'>我屋天之东，月从海西来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197364'>不解传消息，起舞兴悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197364'>千里玉绳断，万顷金波开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197364'>为我清皮骨，怜我兀尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197364'>座有玉山人，欣然共徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197364'>谈笑喜复喜，讵必虾头杯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197364'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_197364_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>还资道斯立诗卷<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197422")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197422'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197422'>秋风吹一叶，送我过东山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197422'>山高日出迟，露重衣裳单。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197422'>爰到济南郡，端士茝与兰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197422'>扁舟八月水，唱酬清且閒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197422'>怜非郭李客，便了取诗看<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：便了，乃斯立童名。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197422'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_197422_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197421?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197421'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197421'>馥馨兰茝语，令人有愧颜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197421'>未见半豹书，安敢道一斑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197421'>分在婢子科，何以能追攀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197421'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_197421_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和斯立见还诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197436")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197436'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197436'>神仙刘子夏，不愧许远游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197436'>今日秋风客，襟度更为优。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197436'>如何琅玕纸，亦作李相投。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197436'>释之还在手，爱涎随不收。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197436'>霜渚望何限，凫鹄远啸俦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197436'>金篦识清扬，玉麈见风流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197436'>新知虽云喜，果作新故<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作胜故知）</span>不。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197436'>相期不用名，散尽人间忧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197436_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197436'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_197436_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和资道读王绩传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197434")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197434'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197434'>飞廉有丑<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作骏）</span>马，卒岁得肥<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作壮）</span>游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197434_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197308'>萧洒裛尘雨，清明避日霓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197308'>露华鸣老鹤，月魄射灵犀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197308'>儒雅元簪笔，风流且带篦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197308'>辛勤无黑突，腾跃有丹梯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197308'>自顾迷辕驾，焉能识路蹊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197308'>从容金谷集，酬唱汉江题。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197308'>好是频徵策，相看便解携。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197308'>尘埃随日起，穷悴使人低。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197308'>桀犬惊尧犬，家鸡笑野鸡。<div id='poem_sentence_11_197308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_197308'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_197308_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和资道登岱顶回</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_196839")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196839'>蔼蔼天孙作晓岚，为嫌俗骨遣教还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196839'>仙儿堕处真堪惜，只在含眸一笑间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　任兖州司法参军。学京氏易，博通五经。作品：《答勾龙寿南先辈书》<div id='poem_1208755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答勾龙寿南先辈书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208755")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208755'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208755'>说之启：古之人教不躐等，学者固不敢躐等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208755_comment'></div>子贡见师乙，问宜何歌，曰：「宜歌商，宜歌齐，宜歌颂，宜歌大雅、小雅、风」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208755_comment'></div>是之谓等，孜孜安弦而后安诗，然后安礼，孰可得而踰哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208755_comment'></div>吾年三十而五，经立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208755_comment'></div>譬之不艺五谷而非上农，不殖百货则非大贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208755_comment'></div>今学者知自置于经师，而不知有人师，甘心为一经之士，名曰大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208755_comment'></div>而实以碎义困踬童子，起而语《易》，薄乎《诗》、《书》，例诋先贤为腐儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208755_comment'></div>先贤说虽是而未新也，颇谓仁义之用，不及道德之恍惚，有愧性命之微妙，但未敢明以孔氏下乎老庄耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208755_comment'></div>然黜《春秋》而尊尚伪《周礼》，弃《孝经》而以《孟子》配《论语》，几何不使文武之道坠地也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208755_comment'></div>足下于此何为超忽世俗，独知所学哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208755_comment'></div>甚善甚善！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208755_comment'></div>而于不肖，猥以长书辩论《孟子》，似亦躐等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208755_comment'></div>足下何不《孝经》、《论语》、《诗》、《书》、《仪礼》、《易》、《春秋》之问，而《孟子》之问乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208755_comment'></div>足下远质《孟子》于荀卿、王充及韩退之晚年之论，近观温公之《疑孟》、李泰伯之《孟子杂辩》、刘元甫之于瞽叟杀人、刘道原之于舜禹避丹均，则世俗孔孟之称安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208755_comment'></div>亦尝一日近思乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208755_comment'></div>何烦足下远过老仆羁旅之舍，而不自珍其辞章乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208755_comment'></div>说之前日叨为太子詹事，请太子读《论语》，而未读《孟子》，所以尊孔子，而尊太子之问学，尚一德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208755_comment'></div>赖陛下明圣，朝奏而暮画可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208755_comment'></div>然卿士大夫骇谤，太学诸生纷纷诬毁百出，无异报私雠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208755_comment'></div>今日放逐之中，尚复何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208755_comment'></div>足下幸察，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208755_comment'></div>正月二十六日，说之上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1208755_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　任兖州司法参军。<br /></div>
-----end

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　二月在蔡州。有诗与江子和兄弟唱和。作品：《赠江子和兄弟》<div id='poem_197593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197593' class='poemTitle -----title
邯郸（武安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6b75a008f0794421bede68090f651774_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b75a008f0794421bede68090f651774");'><span id='6b75a008f0794421bede68090f651774_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1102')">1100-1102年</a>，42-44岁</div><div id='6b75a008f0794421bede68090f651774' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　四月十四日，祷雨紫山回，闻韩相公拜。作品：《君莫恶行》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　五月作文。作品：《恭伯楼记》<div id='poem_1208992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荣伯楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208992")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208992'>武安，鼓山藩其前，太医山殿其后，紫山岌其左，百尖山峘其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208992_comment'></div>厜㕒崷崒，骆驲连属，若断而续，薄于太行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208992_comment'></div>其中大川四五，小川七八，达于漳，入于河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208992_comment'></div>凡赵国之建郡县，皆在桑枣平野，未有武安比，宜夫人物擅山川之秀，多闻人，乃自古寂寞无传至于今，何邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208992_comment'></div>或曰：武安之水多伏流，非若淮济之类中伏而卒大发，其伏遂绝不出矣，得非其故欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208992_comment'></div>或曰非也，有人焉，象其山隐水伏，不自表襮，世人未之知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208992_comment'></div>予求之于古，得高行一人曰台佟孝威，得大儒一人曰马光荣伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208992_comment'></div>荣伯，隋开皇中六儒之冠也，其五人者或死或逐，独荣伯显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208992_comment'></div>文帝幸国子学，荣伯以博士升坐讲《礼》，甚洪赡，论者莫测浅深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208992_comment'></div>当时以次论难者十馀辈，皆一时硕学之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208992_comment'></div>山东三《礼》学，自熊安生后，唯宗荣伯一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208992_comment'></div>荣伯初教授瀛、博间，门徒千数，后多负笈从荣伯长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208992_comment'></div>荣伯在国子学数年，丁母忧，归武安故里，以疾卒，此非其人也邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208992_comment'></div>予既以孝威名轩，自致予之志，又以荣伯名其楼，劝邑子知务学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208992_comment'></div>邑子顾将曰：马荣伯死且数百岁矣，县令贤其人，想其风彩如在，以其人名楼而式之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208992_comment'></div>我辈苟自进，与荣伯比，岂不美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208992_comment'></div>往时虽有一二人华吾邑，而来者烝然秀出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208992_comment'></div>若夫客至登楼四望，如与荣伯游，而觉山川意象，徘徊相高者，其乐又未易可道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208992_comment'></div>元符三年五月日，嵩阳晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1208992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　十一月寄诗陈师道。作品：《无己初除正字以诗寄之》诗。<div id='poem_197351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>无己初除正字以诗寄之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197351")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197351'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197351'>平生阮步兵，口不道臧否。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197351'>每笑谢著作，自是雌黄口。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197351'>闭门秋草多，金风摇白昼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197351'>忽传黄纸书，校艺群公后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197351'>执雁有楚越，佩剑无左右。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197351'>难<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>画浑沌眉，遽识齐宿瘤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197351'>彭城陈夫子，笑我颜何厚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197351'>为语陈夫子，人生无不有。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197351'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_197351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197351'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_197351_0'>⑴ 原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197351_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在磁州武安任上，作《易规》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在磁州武安任上，作《题古周易后》<div id='poem_1208800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题古周易后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208800")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208800'>《周易》卦爻一，《彖》二，《象》三，《文言》四，《系辞》五，《说卦》六，《序卦》七，《杂卦》八，缮写谨第如上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208800_comment'></div>按晋太康初，发汲县旧冢，得古简编蝌蚪文字，散乱不可训知，独《周易》最为明了，上下篇与今正同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208800_comment'></div>有阴阳说而无《彖》、《象》、《文言》、《系辞》，杜预疑于时仲尼造之于鲁，尚未播之远国，而《汉艺文志》《易经》十二篇，施、孟、梁丘三家，颜师古曰：「上下经及十翼，故十二篇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208800_comment'></div>是则《彖》、《象》、《文言》、《系辞》始附卦爻而传于汉欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208800_comment'></div>先儒谓费直专以《彖》、《象》、《文言》参解《易》爻，以《彖》、《象》、《文言》杂入卦中者，自费氏始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208800_comment'></div>其初费氏不列学官，唯行民间，至汉末陈元方、郑康成之徒皆学费氏，古十二篇之《易》遂亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208800_comment'></div>孔颖达又谓辅嗣之意，《象》本释经，宜相附近，分爻之《象》辞各附当爻，则费氏初变乱古制时，犹若今《乾卦》，《彖》、《象》系卦之末欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208800_comment'></div>古经始变于费氏，而卒大乱于王弼，惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208800_comment'></div>奈何后之儒生尤而效之，杜预分《左氏传》于经，宋衷、范望辈散《太玄》、《赞》与《测》于八十一首，是其明比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208800_comment'></div>揆观厥初，乃如古文《尚书》，司马迁、班固《序传》，扬雄《法言·序篇》云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208800_comment'></div>今民间《法言》列《序篇》于其篇首，与学官书不同，概可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208800_comment'></div>唐李鼎祚又取《序卦》冠之卦首，则又效小王之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208800_comment'></div>今悉还其初，庶几学者不执《彖》以徇卦，不执《象》以徇爻云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208800_comment'></div>昔韩宣子适鲁见《易》象，是古人以卦爻统名之曰象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208800_comment'></div>故曰《易》之象也，其意深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208800_comment'></div>岂若后之人卦必以象明，象必以辞显，纷纷多岐哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208800_comment'></div>呜呼，学者曾未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208800_comment'></div>刘牧云：「小《象》独《乾》不系于爻辞，尊君也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208800_comment'></div>石守道亦曰：「孔子作《彖》、《象》于六爻之前，小《象》系逐爻之下，惟《乾》悉属之于后者，让也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208800_comment'></div>呜呼，他人尚何责哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208800_comment'></div>若夫文字之传，始有齐楚之异音，卒有科斗籀篆隶书之四变，因而讹谬者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208800_comment'></div>刘向尝以中古文《易》经校施、孟、梁丘经，至蜀李撰又尝著《古文易》，则今之所传者皆非古文也，安得睹夫刘、李之书乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208800_comment'></div>其幸而诸儒之传，今有所稽考者，具列其异同舛讹于字下，亦庶几乎同复于古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208800_comment'></div>或曰：子能古文，何不古文写之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208800_comment'></div>曰：有改于华而无变于实者，予不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208800_comment'></div>如古者竹简重大，以经为二篇，今又何必以二篇成帙哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208800_comment'></div>谨录而藏诸，以俟博古君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208800_comment'></div>建中靖国元年辛巳五月二十四日，嵩山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1208800_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　因元符末应诏封事落邪中等。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
无极（无极县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='dc08540143f640d7bbe28e50fcae730f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dc08540143f640d7bbe28e50fcae730f");'><span id='dc08540143f640d7bbe28e50fcae730f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>，45岁</div><div id='dc08540143f640d7bbe28e50fcae730f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>改承议郎，知定州无极县，有政绩，建问山堂。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>友韩瑨在保州建娱山堂，说之为作记。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>六月作《爱萱堂记》作品：《娱山堂记》<div id='poem_1208993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>娱山堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208993")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208993'>予读谢康乐《山居赋》，见其所称「杭顶葺馆，殷峰启轩，呈美表趣，百种错出若图然」，辄叹夫境胜于情，外有所慕，而超然独往之愿迨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208993_comment'></div>迨陶渊明赋《归去来》，虽颇道山川登临之胜，及其所居则环堵萧然，不蔽风日，其深自爱者，不过绕屋之树，中园之蔬，且曰「山气日夕佳」耳，一何简易耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208993_comment'></div>何所往而不得其乐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208993_comment'></div>若渊明者真有乐于山水，而不待山水以为乐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208993_comment'></div>顾视康乐静寿之德，不其惭欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208993_comment'></div>塞北之狼山，无岞崿峭茜可喜之姿，令人瞩寓，惟是古昔干戈战斗之场，与夫沃盬之所，栖界乎阴山羯胡之域，非道家所谓洞天福地，而莫睹夫高人隐士之遗躅，寿草灵兽，亦未知或生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208993_comment'></div>孤宦远客，每览夫四时积雪，而不胜飘零之感也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208993_comment'></div>颍川韩君表倅保州，新其堂，瞰狼山而独乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208993_comment'></div>夫既自得于清音矣，必欲极其志尚，又取古今画手阴岩阳壑脱绘于屋壁，朝夕寝食，启处便是山间，不知狼山之果美恶于壁山之真幻，名之曰娱山堂，得非有乐于山水，而不待山水以为乐者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208993_comment'></div>君表，少师诸孙，有别第在颍川，嵩少箕隗乃其家山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208993_comment'></div>初仕杭州幕府，穷极吴越山水矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208993_comment'></div>自杭来保塞，乃不怒憎而乐焉如此，盖非厌常欣暂者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208993_comment'></div>说之早怀嵩少卜筑之志，贫未能即日行也，闻君表之新堂，恨不相与从容于其上，敢辞拒不为之记？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208993_comment'></div>崇宁二年癸未四月乙丑，嵩阳晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1208993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>王安中尝师事晁说之。作品：《爱萱堂记》<div id='poem_1208994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>爱萱堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208994")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208994'>中山在战国时，近介于燕赵，远距诸韩魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208994_comment'></div>其土地不足以当十之一，其积粟器械不足以当十之二，其君不知谓谁而足以强其国，其谋臣不知为谁而相与致一时之盛，其势隐然韩魏燕赵之敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208994_comment'></div>惜古史不存，莫可得详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208994_comment'></div>唐自天宝末，大河之北跋扈不轨，无复君臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208994_comment'></div>逮夫广明、中和间，义武王处存者乃独效微忠于盗贼崎岖之际，盖常山之灵常卫之，从陶唐氏为侯国，时故都自有所资也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208994_comment'></div>本朝名公伟人作镇，光辉晔晔，接躅雄天下，不特号天下劲兵处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208994_comment'></div>自忠献魏公而来，其治尚简易敦大，胡虏因知王国之尊，慕德慑伏，而兵肃民安乐无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208994_comment'></div>或苟失是选，则众哗然跼蹐，虽劳无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208994_comment'></div>朝夕箕栉，视一小侯无异，失朝廷所以倚重之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208994_comment'></div>以故魏公之绩绘诸丹青，乡人庙祀，岁时唯谨不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208994_comment'></div>其所建阅古堂，亦雄天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208994_comment'></div>彼江湖淮汉间，非无危楼杰观，擅山川之丽，环奇清之赏，而于是不得亢其传也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208994_comment'></div>江夏黄公镇治数月，作堂于阅古之东南，栋楹梴桷，则不敢移前人，而名之曰爱萱堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208994_comment'></div>惟公自登进士第，即显于朝，蒙累圣之知，日侍太夫人食饮，康强如壮年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208994_comment'></div>不惜金帛，重赏劝功，前日疲驽，亦克拳捍蹶张，无一饭无宾客，从容文史歌诗壶觞之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208994_comment'></div>凡其施为举措，独得于上心，良可乐矣，尚何所事而萱之爱哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208994_comment'></div>岂非公之所乐者众能知之，而公之所忧，众不足以与知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208994_comment'></div>且自谓所治未至简易敦大，而恐古今闻人之羞乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208994_comment'></div>不然，小物也，公亦爱之而不忘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208994_comment'></div>不然，则卫之诗人所思者自有所在，而传者谬曰令人忘忧也邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208994_comment'></div>嵇叔夜之爱吾萱者往矣，复何足道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208994_comment'></div>客或以是意请于公，公曰：「吾园中多萱耳，吾不知其他」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208994_comment'></div>说之闻而叹曰：「伟哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208994_comment'></div>记之以待知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208994_comment'></div>崇宁二年癸未夏六月戊辰，承议郎、知无极县事兼兵马都监、武骑尉、赐绯鱼袋晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1208994_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
河南
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b64d32c410304be1a1857b5e2dfed9ed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b64d32c410304be1a1857b5e2dfed9ed");'><span id='b64d32c410304be1a1857b5e2dfed9ed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1106')">1104-1106年</a>，46-48岁</div><div id='b64d32c410304be1a1857b5e2dfed9ed' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　被劾罢，领嵩山中岳庙祠禄，隐居嵩山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　此后三四年间，每年入洛省亲旧于司马光家及范祖禹家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　四月作文。作品：《王氏双松堂记》<div id='poem_1208995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王氏双松堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208995")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208995'>昔夏后初都阳城，南踰洛阳百里而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208995_comment'></div>成汤迁亳殷，东踰洛阳五十里而近，皆舍洛阳而不都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208995_comment'></div>周兴，武王既定鼎郏鄏，厥后召公宅洛邑，周公营成周，其意盛矣，而成王卒不果迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208995_comment'></div>逮夫宣王中兴，自镐之洛，狩于圃田，及于敖山，因以朝诸侯，《车攻》之诗作焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208995_comment'></div>岂不欲成周、召之志欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208995_comment'></div>且宣王尝狩于岐，而石鼓之诗亦伟矣，夫子乃舍而不录，得非岐之狩为常，而东都之狩非常乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208995_comment'></div>惜夫宣王卒，亦不果迁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208995_comment'></div>至平王是迁而周衰矣，尚复何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208995_comment'></div>唯是三代之盛所遗而不飨者，气象轇轕，轮囷郁然，发而不施，山含辉而馀秀，川澄渊而轶润，草木得之异态日新，其在风俗逸豫安舒，特宜搢绅先生潜养之适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208995_comment'></div>盖自李耳为周柱下史而来，风流高矣而远不胜道，姑以近世三人者识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208995_comment'></div>唐卢仝之隐，不资嵩高少室之雄而近在城阙之中，草屋数间，闭门不出者以岁纪论，微韩愈殆莫知其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208995_comment'></div>哀帝时宰相杨涉之子凝式，于学无不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208995_comment'></div>尝谏其父亡唐而复臣相梁，不得志，因阳狂一时，终五代贤者诛戮不自保之际，逸乐白首，其中盖有大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208995_comment'></div>观其丹青遗像，知其为伟丈夫，而笔墨之妙，凛然生气犹在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208995_comment'></div>自庆历来，康节先生邵尧夫贫居天津之南，独明先圣之道，不老不释，卓然振千古之绝学，颇苦志著书，而精深难窥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208995_comment'></div>天子尝命之官，不得辞而身不出，公卿大夫乐从之游，而莫能名其器，既死而名益高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208995_comment'></div>夫此三人者唯洛阳之宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208995_comment'></div>所谓逸豫安舒之风，盖可观已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208995_comment'></div>呜呼，名有帝王山川之胜，而实宜夫高人处士之奉，坐通四海九州之凑，何其盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208995_comment'></div>以故公卿大夫功成得谢，危楼杰观、水竹花卉之丽甲天下，而不以为侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208995_comment'></div>绳枢瓮牖之生，终日欣然，亦自以为得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208995_comment'></div>孰非所宜者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208995_comment'></div>王君圣徒庭鲤世为洛人，躬筑别墅建春门里，植双松以自见其志，因以双松名其堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208995_comment'></div>日与平生故人徜徉图画壶觞之乐，四方之宾客如归焉，靡不适可，且自叹曰：「吾老矣，恐不得如吾松之寿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208995_comment'></div>而吾之志，则不可不著之异日」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208995_comment'></div>于是恳予文以记于石，予因道古今之所以然者书之，使后之游者得以赏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208995_comment'></div>崇宁四年四月十七日，嵩高晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1208995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　六月大病，作文。作品：《祭麴神文》<div id='poem_1209059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭曲神文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1209059")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209059'>维崇宁四年乙酉六月上寅，谨用茶果祭于五方土公、曲王、曲人曰：主人性不饮酒，无寸长于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209059_comment'></div>使举世中，皆如主人，周难多忧，浩不必陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209059_comment'></div>惶惶所困，曷云今晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209059_comment'></div>敬式古法，不违吉辰，匪他之求，疾病是轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209059_comment'></div>五金八石，明朱空青，虽立起死，如主人贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209059_comment'></div>门冬昌术，尚戚不仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209059_comment'></div>一有疾病，四声入邻，多空手归，妻侮女嗔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209059_comment'></div>欲自效力，唯我曲王曲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209059_comment'></div>五更凄露，辘轳苦辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209059_comment'></div>前期白曲，亦未能先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209059_comment'></div>二物既备，屏气逡巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209059_comment'></div>妇女不见，鸡犬不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209059_comment'></div>炉丸之丹，异品同勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209059_comment'></div>念尔有神，吉祥其臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209059_comment'></div>辄复自怜，废弃三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209059_comment'></div>每饥不饱，此又胡然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209059_comment'></div>禹迹之中，无片瓦椽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209059_comment'></div>我笔我墨，赁屋于山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209059_comment'></div>听泉枕石，肠胃亦填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209059_comment'></div>一杯之饭，沙砾相缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209059_comment'></div>离娄如瞽，易牙不贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209059_comment'></div>盖亦有道，牛龁而咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209059_comment'></div>吁其已久，腰坠足颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209059_comment'></div>瘿滋瓮盎，溲亦涩涓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209059_comment'></div>苟弗消除，我危特艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209059_comment'></div>然是末尔，何足多理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209059_comment'></div>念尔有神，救其大厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209059_comment'></div>刚肠斯柔，尚可富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209059_comment'></div>无信古人，大言远视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209059_comment'></div>此誉而誉，彼毁而毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209059_comment'></div>笑语妩好，谁复我鄙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209059_comment'></div>沈绝旧学，不到唇齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209059_comment'></div>远人书疏，蚕头谨字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209059_comment'></div>近人请谒，百门千纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209059_comment'></div>炎炎先附，寂寂卑退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209059_comment'></div>用间于亲，厚我百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209059_comment'></div>傅罪于贤，功亦不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209059_comment'></div>一朝鸿禧，复使职位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209059_comment'></div>东海搜珠，西海筑垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209059_comment'></div>南海刲龙，北海缚鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209059_comment'></div>入拜宗工，先媚涕泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209059_comment'></div>载言盛德，有前莫比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209059_comment'></div>古称皋夔，今百执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209059_comment'></div>谁冥司命，亦未必我死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209059_comment'></div>爰积愆尤，四十七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209059_comment'></div>悔过自惩，从今日始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209059_comment'></div>急急如律令。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1209059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1209059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　与陈恬同隐于嵩山。作品：《闻叔易隐居被召》二首。<div id='poem_196911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻叔易隐居被召二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：亡一。按：另一首见后辑补）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_196911")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196911'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196911'>处士何人为作牙，尽携猿鹤到京华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196911'>故山岩壑应惆怅，六六峰前只一家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196911'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196911_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　康与之尝从晁说之问学。作品：《雨霁闻溪流作》<div id='poem_197310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雨霁闻溪流作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197310")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_197310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197310'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197310'>山前霖雨霁，流水兴何长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197310'>曲涧通兰若，馀音到草堂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197310'>龙鳞应已备，鱼尾得令狂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197310'>奏凯入关阵，寻仙泛海航。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197310'>月添波荡漾，风共影㳽茫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197310'>不作羁臣泪，明朝涸复常。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197310_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197310'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_197310_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　隐居嵩山作诗。作品：《峻极上院》<div id='poem_196921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196921' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196921?labeling=true' target='_blank'>峻极上院</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_196921")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196921_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196921'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196921'>山下青青春已归，百花山上正芳菲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196921'>人间颜色易零落，百万千年云锦衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196921'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196921_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　正月，党禁除。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　五月，为江子和作墓志铭。作品：《江子和墓志铭》<div id='poem_1209037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江子和墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1209037")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209037'>君讳端礼，字子和，一字季恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209037_comment'></div>始江氏自汉轑阳侯德为陈留圉城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209037_comment'></div>祖讳休复，仁宗时修起居注，有重名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209037_comment'></div>考讳懋相，朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209037_comment'></div>子和生而沈粹，年十七游太学，为同辈敬惮，独裕然不肯就公试，或试则居上列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209037_comment'></div>常叹曰：「是不足学也，令人惭耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209037_comment'></div>方是时，东坡谪居黄州，子和特倾慕之，以书讲学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209037_comment'></div>子和于一世德名人皆愿从之游，闻人毫发之善，汲汲称道，惟恐不及，盖自其舍人之风流为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209037_comment'></div>子和学诗律于黄鲁直，论经行于徐仲车为尤谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209037_comment'></div>二公俱以子和为贤，此二公者，他人或不能并善其家法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209037_comment'></div>方举世不为《春秋》之学时，有六合崔子方伯直者，世莫知其为人，子和一见而定交，曰：「此吾之所学也，愿与子共之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209037_comment'></div>伯直遂因子和得名于诸公间，子和之志行远矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209037_comment'></div>其事亲孝，能色养，教二弟必欲与己同善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209037_comment'></div>然诺谨于仆妾，不侮乎童稚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209037_comment'></div>终日在闇室无惰容，如天使而寿且仕宦，得时为祭酒，为御史大夫，劝讲金华则优矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209037_comment'></div>不幸年三十有八，以绍圣四年七月二十三日疫不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209037_comment'></div>娶王氏，能为子和躬劳苦，先子和卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209037_comment'></div>再娶张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209037_comment'></div>子男三人，女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209037_comment'></div>其二弟端友、端本，今俱以文行称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209037_comment'></div>二弟裒子和之遗藁为集若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209037_comment'></div>子和尝病柳子厚作《非国语》，乃作《非非国语》，东坡见之曰：「久有意为此书，不谓君先之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209037_comment'></div>鲁直则曰：「子和文辞简理似尹师鲁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209037_comment'></div>以崇宁五年五月十五日从葬于阳夏先墓之次，崔六合为行状，黄州潘邠老欲铭之，而邠老卒，宛丘张文潜又欲为铭，会文潜病，不果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209037_comment'></div>说之六弟微之光道与子和早相善，因得子和在兄弟间，乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1209037'>天何为哉嘻善士，植植方茂忽以逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209037_comment'></div>不使究极能厥世，或如好之聊嬉戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209037_comment'></div>彼顽凶狠天亦畏，一既生之莫敢毙，又且富贵如其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209037_comment'></div>子和九原何所遗，汉轑阳侯百世嗣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1209037_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
芮城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5f698cf6e5c449b3b029c93b9f1add71_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5f698cf6e5c449b3b029c93b9f1add71");'><span id='5f698cf6e5c449b3b029c93b9f1add71_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1107')">1106-1107年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='5f698cf6e5c449b3b029c93b9f1add71' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　冬，监陕州集津仓。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　六月，长子卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　冬，罢官，领华山西岳庙祠禄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　十一月，作文论及易学。作品：《传易堂记》<div id='poem_1208996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>传易堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208996")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208996'>古者六艺之学必谨师授，其称是人经明有家法，至东都犹甚严也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208996_comment'></div>鲁商瞿子木受《易》孔子，五传而至汉齐田何子装，汉之《易》家盖自田何始，何而上未尝有书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208996_comment'></div>魏管辂谓《易》安可注者，其得先儒之心欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208996_comment'></div>古今学者咸谓卜子夏受《易》孔子而为之传，然太史公、刘向父子、班固皆不论著，唐刘子玄知其伪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208996_comment'></div>是书亡不传于今，今号为《子夏易传》者，《崇文总目》亦斥其非是，而不知其所作之人，予知其为唐张弧之《易》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208996_comment'></div>是子夏亦未尝有书，而以《易》之道教授西河，其后汾晋之间《易》以故特盛欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208996_comment'></div>汉自田何授东武王同、洛阳周王孙、丁宽、齐服生四人者，乃始为之传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208996_comment'></div>然王氏、周氏、服氏书各二篇，丁氏八篇，亦不过训诂举大义云耳，岂为巧慧组绣之靡也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208996_comment'></div>而《易》家著书则自王同始，同授淄川杨何，所谓「易杨」者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208996_comment'></div>丁宽授砀田王孙，王孙授沛施雠、东海孟喜、琅邪梁丘贺三家，又皆列于学官，最为盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208996_comment'></div>其弟子颛门者众，厥后又有东郡京房之学亦得立，而学官则自杨何始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208996_comment'></div>又其后有东莱费直之《易》，有沛高相之《易》，唯传民间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208996_comment'></div>此三家者虽户牖不同，而堂奥之安则一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208996_comment'></div>盖皆兼三才，而备错总极变通焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208996_comment'></div>房谓其学即孟氏学，相自言出于丁将军，讵弗信耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208996_comment'></div>惟费氏之传晚而益盛，东都陈元、郑众、马融、郑玄、荀爽、魏王肃、王弼皆其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208996_comment'></div>自肃而上，莫敢悖其所传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208996_comment'></div>唯弼年少，厌旧喜新，乃一切摈弃师法，攘庄老恍惚虚无之论，专于人事，以快后生耳目，而称为《易》之妙，乃不知《易》之奥妙自有所在，而无用庄老汨之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208996_comment'></div>譬之惰农乞市以饱，而弗顾南亩之可耘耔，惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208996_comment'></div>《易》之杂乎庄老而专明人事，则自王弼始，《易》家乃始失其所传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208996_comment'></div>梁丘、施、孟三家于是乎亡于晋，而孟氏、京氏有书无师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208996_comment'></div>属江左祖尚玄虚，弼之学滋得以盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208996_comment'></div>然其初，虞翻传其家五世孟氏之学，为时推重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208996_comment'></div>晋王庾虽喜清谈，而专立郑学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208996_comment'></div>干宝辈犹不忘乎京氏，而孙盛诋弼之傅会浮丽，又已力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208996_comment'></div>宋元嘉欲矜学校之盛，而王、郑两立，逮颜延之为祭酒而黜郑置王，齐之王学遂大盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208996_comment'></div>陆澄《贻王俭书》云：「《易》自商瞿之后，虽有异家之学，同以象数为宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208996_comment'></div>数年后乃有王弼之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208996_comment'></div>王济云，弼所误者多，何必能顿废前儒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208996_comment'></div>予赏味其言，未尝不三叹息之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208996_comment'></div>时王俭在位，善澄之言，于是学者略知郑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208996_comment'></div>至梁何胤之徒，又窃释氏空有所能异端而誇于弼，斯又弼之罪人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208996_comment'></div>其在河北诸儒，则专祖郑氏，所谓衣冠礼乐尽在中原者，此亦其躅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208996_comment'></div>不幸隋兴，缙绅学士反浮丽是慕，弼之学遂为中原之师，而唐因之，于是乎《易》家古法始泯灭无闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208996_comment'></div>然隋汾晋之间有仲长子光、关子明、王仲华、王通辈，传《易》自有指归，不失乎古，得非子夏之遗风哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208996_comment'></div>盖汉严君平、扬子云、魏管辂、晋郭璞、孙登、隋关朗、唐僧一行、玄真子、张志和，其于《易》又特最深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208996_comment'></div>是谓一世伟人，非有所待而兴，亦莫得而沮溺之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208996_comment'></div>至有宋，华山希夷先生陈抟图南以《易》授终南种徵君放明逸，明逸授汶阳穆参军脩伯长，而武功苏舜钦子美亦尝从伯长学，伯长授青州李之才挺之，挺之授河南邵康节先生雍尧夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208996_comment'></div>惟康节先生天资既卓越不群，而夜不施枕，惟《易》之学者三十年，其兼三才而错总变通之妙始大著明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208996_comment'></div>自希夷而来，皆未尝有书，乃如子木、子夏之初欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208996_comment'></div>有庐江范谔昌者，亦尝受《易》于种徵君，谔昌授彭城刘牧，而聱隅先生黄晞及陈纯臣之徒，皆由范氏知名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208996_comment'></div>其于康节之《易》，源委初同，而浅深不伦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208996_comment'></div>华山旧有希夷先生祠堂，而种徵君实关辅之望，后之好事者并以绘徵君之像，山中有隐者又知传《易》之所自，而并康节先生之像绘焉，榜之曰传易堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208996_comment'></div>游是山者，徘徊俯仰三峰万仞之峥嵘崷崒，其意壮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208996_comment'></div>及登斯堂，睹三先生之貌，耸然加敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208996_comment'></div>逖观上古圣人画卦之本意，而知夫防忧患于几微，身与《易》准，则向之所揽者又将忘之矣，不亦伟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208996_comment'></div>是堂之传，其与山镇俱不朽欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208996_comment'></div>康节先生之子伯温以说之服勤康节之学，俾为之记，不得辞，乃具道《易》之授受本末、兴废得失之由，以尊三先生之道，亦且效藏诸名山之意云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208996_comment'></div>大观元年丁亥十有一月甲戌，嵩山晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1208996_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宁波
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3ef6ca48296c434d9fc09ab2e6a563c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3ef6ca48296c434d9fc09ab2e6a563c3");'><span id='3ef6ca48296c434d9fc09ab2e6a563c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1113')">1110-1113年</a>，52-55岁</div><div id='3ef6ca48296c434d9fc09ab2e6a563c3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　冬，赴任监明州船场。与欧阳修子欧阳棐游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　在明州，四月，祭友文。作品：《祭邹志完文》<div id='poem_1209056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209056?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭邹志完文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1209056")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209056'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209056'>维政和元年岁次辛卯，四月壬子，具官晁说之谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于志完侍郎同年之灵：惟公生而纯明，玉未琢而先白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209056_comment'></div>美早成而众誉，方思畜而躬积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209056_comment'></div>念不屈于小官，矧得申于黼席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209056_comment'></div>知所言之如何，安自刚乎胆策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209056_comment'></div>谁行堪乎岭南，乃连岁而再役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209056_comment'></div>后皇仁而可忧，入瘴雾而不瘠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209056_comment'></div>方湛恩于里闬，何疾病而易箦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209056_comment'></div>嗟无恙于投荒，而不起于安宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209056_comment'></div>知非人之毒君，是惟君之自螫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209056_comment'></div>君神定而长髯，若星官与羽客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209056_comment'></div>虽不达于人间，犹龄松而齿石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209056_comment'></div>忽舍老母而下世，年才踰乎半百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209056_comment'></div>既疾病而融融，独顾母而唶唶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209056_comment'></div>乡人当君之斯时，候问疲而接迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209056_comment'></div>相率佞佛佞道，身可赎而谁惜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209056_comment'></div>竟不验于须臾，徒垂泪于窀穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209056_comment'></div>率是一乡之情，在四海而无射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209056_comment'></div>盖云畜于石中，雨为天下之泽，众有望而不符，君志又亦奚获？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209056_comment'></div>行路恸而此及，我独侘傺之剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209056_comment'></div>顾惟北方之学，不老隐而佛颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209056_comment'></div>敢出位以新奇，仁义自乎开辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209056_comment'></div>君每幼服而叹，曰高论之如掷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209056_comment'></div>我方贻书以勉此，云何生死之隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209056_comment'></div>闻君疾病而异梦，恍惚帝所之履舄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209056_comment'></div>得非所忧之深，遂自达其所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209056_comment'></div>不然岚虺之馀，使君蛊而神癖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209056_comment'></div>呜呼沈痛之何诉，君有子如圭璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209056_comment'></div>庶君后之必大，亘流光而有赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209056_comment'></div>君真今日之死耶，我之生亦何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209056_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1209056_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　与吕好问往还，念及好文诸子。作《申刘》一篇，辨舜河南事。<div id='poem_1208970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申刘</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208970")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208970'>说之十馀年来始不惑于孟子，为之辩正，大端自谓悉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208970_comment'></div>及见刘道原说「月正元日，舜格于文祖」，是尧崩踰年事，不待三年丧毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208970_comment'></div>其斥孟子甚明，且罪孔安国仍轲之缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208970_comment'></div>乃大耸叹恨，不得道原而在北面师事焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208970_comment'></div>然道原意有所遗者辄申之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208970_comment'></div>尧知其子不肖，不足以传天下，幸而得舜以授之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208970_comment'></div>舜既摄二十八载之久矣，乃复待尧三年丧毕，避之南河之南，是尧之子才足以传天下欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208970_comment'></div>尧远能知舜而近于其子则不知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208970_comment'></div>贼父子之恩而渎君臣之分，孰大于此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208970_comment'></div>尧苟不知其子，舜乃独知之，为舜者曷不让之于摄政之初，使尧见之乃有待毕三年之丧，即位之初，弃宗庙百官而逝耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208970_comment'></div>无乃舜之是举也伪欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208970_comment'></div>天下至重器，授受至重事，何容伪毫发哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208970_comment'></div>后世乱臣贼子接踵奋袂而起，舜或倡之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208970_comment'></div>舜于是上不诚于尧，下惑斯民，以天下为市而术取之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208970_comment'></div>丹朱不肖子也，一日见舜避之远，乃起而言曰：「天下吾家之世有也，至我始不身之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208970_comment'></div>吾父虽欲授舜，而舜不敢居以避我，我何为不如舜之志也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208970_comment'></div>且舜之志，天下志也，我之受宜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208970_comment'></div>则舜以天下病，而利丹朱一人，岂尧之所以知舜之心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208970_comment'></div>如丹朱曰：「舜之避我虽远，如吾父命何，天下之朝觐狱讼讴歌顾可欺哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208970_comment'></div>必以天下奉舜，是舜非受天下于尧，乃受之丹朱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208970_comment'></div>丹朱不知为舜亦何憾，彼朝觐狱讼者必忿然而争，争必至于兵，丹朱将不保其躯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208970_comment'></div>舜欲利丹朱而实欲杀之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208970_comment'></div>舜之南河之日，天下祸乱肇耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208970_comment'></div>夫既不忍尧之子而避之矣，其之中国，践天子位，则顾众人之情，而不待丹朱之一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208970_comment'></div>不若其初不避之愈，而徒以暴丹朱之不肖耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208970_comment'></div>此非常大事，其后禹、益又皆例之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208970_comment'></div>书虽残编，不应如此大事略无所著见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208970_comment'></div>其荐益事，则温公辩之矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1208970_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　在明州。作品：《癸未岁余与开封解安行通知定州外县……今辛卯……感旧作寄》《政和元年正月一日作》《纪赠法智诗序》《止观妙境辨正》《卢沃字子献序》《跋东坡刚说》<div id='poem_197193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸未岁余与开封解安行同知定州外县赴二帅上元之集今辛卯明州灯夕公会上见邸报解以大夫知嘉州感旧作寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197193")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197193'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197193'>伊昔中山胜事赊，初当三五便开花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197193'>君能选色沉醉倒，我自伤心深感嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197193'>聚散十年逢节序，穷通百态各天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197193'>使君绮席谁同乐，莫遣灯花照鬓华<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：予与解同岁。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197193'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197193_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>政和元年正月一日作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197464")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_197464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197464'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197464'>元年元日日甲子，从自汉历来有三。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197464'>总把皇恩调玉烛，今朝独更觉春酣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197464'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_197464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197464'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_197464_0'>⑴ 自注：东汉、元魏皆是正月一日甲子，与今凡三。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197464_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1208785' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208785' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208785?labeling=true' target='_blank'>纪赠法智诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208785")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208785_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208785'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208785'>今天台教观之徒，称四明尊者追配古人，其言为国中之法也，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208785_comment'></div>说之自北方来，闻而异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208785_comment'></div>究其名氏，是谓法智礼公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208785_comment'></div>于是乎矍然嘉叹曰：此我高祖文元公与杨文公之所称者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208785_comment'></div>我虽昧于天台之学，未读法智所著之书，而固已得其人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208785_comment'></div>既而法智世孙明智立公视以高僧简长等纪赠诗二十三首，曰：「吾祖法智得名凛然至今者，盖有所自矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208785_comment'></div>当是时翰林主人晁公、杨公所贻之文既已流传矣，其辈行中声名人篇章之美又如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208785_comment'></div>然是诗吾与法智初不自有之，乃落于杭州式公，不知其历几岁，凡传几何人，然亦复还归于法智之旧室，亦可叹已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208785_comment'></div>将移于石，欲得以序之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208785_comment'></div>说之以谓法智远处身于东海之陂，而名声振耀于京师，既久而弥隆，其颂德辞翰散而复合，亦可以为修德之劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208785_comment'></div>后有览者，所感可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208785_comment'></div>呜乎，景德祥符之风，此亦非其躅欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208785_comment'></div>政和元年十月庚申，具位晁说之叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1208785_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>止观妙境辩正序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208782")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208782'>予自洛郑间至四明，闻天台之教而喜之，一遇延庆明智讲主立公之论辩而疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208782_comment'></div>未几，倾心愿从事焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208782_comment'></div>然其书万千百言，浩然若巨浸之波涛，难为舳舻之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208782_comment'></div>虽有头数义目，而森然如上穹之万象，孰为盈缩伏留，私窃病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208782_comment'></div>明智曰：「是何忧思之过哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208782_comment'></div>吾祖以一药瘉万病，一句折群言，厉痾立成玉雪之肤，而鼓篁悉叶清商之律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208782_comment'></div>其唯十章乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208782_comment'></div>十章亦夥矣，又乃辟而为十境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208782_comment'></div>十境远矣，运而为十乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208782_comment'></div>十乘或其劳矣，安而为观不思议一境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208782_comment'></div>惟是智者之一境，荆溪因文字而示三境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208782_comment'></div>惜夫晚出好哗，或执为语见，而荡为义路，区区昼夜，分文析字，正堕古人多盐少豉之讥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208782_comment'></div>予每闻其言，欲以笔墨记之，内顾未究其学，不敢自诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208782_comment'></div>颇疑明智有所著之书，问焉，笑不复答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208782_comment'></div>久之，乃见《摩诃止观妙境辩正》一编于其学徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208782_comment'></div>伏读累日，乃叹其既妙于讲论，又善乎著述，不矜不耀之为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208782_comment'></div>余之知若人者甚微，其所不知者尚多也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208782_comment'></div>乃责其学徒曰：「若辈得珍羞而闭门，不以饱满众人欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208782_comment'></div>乃请余序而刊诸板。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208782_comment'></div>顾予何知焉，窃因是书将忘智者之一，宁论荆溪之三哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208782_comment'></div>盖一源为观不思议境，而派之为三，曰性德、修德、化他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208782_comment'></div>学者当守一源而澄清乎，抑亦浮其派而泛滥乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208782_comment'></div>且其一云者，不得已而指之也，又从而三焉，果不得已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208782_comment'></div>抑亦可以已而不已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208782_comment'></div>荆溪之义例，又于是境立五例四意，学者何谓独谨此三而慢五焉与四乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208782_comment'></div>果从荆溪之笃论乎，抑亦因文字而不得已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208782_comment'></div>请以荆溪之语语乎荆溪，不曰性修不二乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208782_comment'></div>孰谓荆溪而自矛盾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208782_comment'></div>要当师智者一人，观不思议一境，是乃为辩正云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208782_comment'></div>宜先之以智者及荆溪之书，次以广智及正公、义公之诸说，终之以辩正，使学者得以考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208782_comment'></div>政和元年辛卯十一月癸未，嵩山晁说之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1208782_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卢沃字子献序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208987")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208987'>四明卢沃少字天启，长为古学，所志简易，忽叹曰：「古之人名若隐而显，其字抑而不侈，孔门弟子如何，我岂不愧诸」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208987_comment'></div>乃请更字于嵩山晁说之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208987_comment'></div>说之谢曰：子穷无以饱妻子，朝夕而寒不敢辞，作为文章数百千轴，而写无纸笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208987_comment'></div>意欲领略，上极太史公之所不载，下尽欧阳公之所遗，使经纬不相杂糅，视彼父康成而兄子慎者，欲唾而奴之，尚谁可与朋侪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208987_comment'></div>孰不能一官，而徬徨十年，无路以进？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208987_comment'></div>今幸得试礼部，冒霜雪，绝江淮，辛苦数千里之涂，书一束外，艰得一钱，乃无世俗觊觎之色，而思古人之似耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208987_comment'></div>甚哉，子之进矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208987_comment'></div>子谓高宗、傅说启心沃心之事，岂有异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208987_comment'></div>是君之所宜望于其臣者，而臣之职当然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208987_comment'></div>为人臣而苟知所职，则有死无不言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208987_comment'></div>学者误谈信而后谏，相率为容身持禄之计，不知所谓信耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208987_comment'></div>若彼孟子所谓惟大人为能格君心之非者，孟子周流不遇，疾愤群小在位，一时之言，身无自恕，曰我欲献忠，如非大人何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208987_comment'></div>不过时有难易，子如与房、杜、王、魏为僚事太宗，则进说何难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208987_comment'></div>或不幸而同诸邺侯、宣公，区区剀切德宗，斯诚艰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208987_comment'></div>然又有难者，我艺祖谓人君以纳谏为美，何如自不为非，不劳臣下谏诤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208987_comment'></div>当是之时，虽赵韩王无谋谟之迹，诛卢绛而诸将征伐愈武，不用杨徽之而群臣德业益厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208987_comment'></div>子之献纳于斯时，弗益艰欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208987_comment'></div>子仕矣，愿且勉诸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208987_comment'></div>无谓傅岩一老曰能，敢字子曰子献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208987_comment'></div>政和元年辛巳十一月辛丑序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1208987_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋东坡刚说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208808")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208808'>东坡甲戌年后诗文，说之所见不少矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208808_comment'></div>今日乃始见《刚说》于明州，令人不觉意气自倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208808_comment'></div>鲁直字画亦云刚矣，而李端叔者辄有疵评，是方竹可削，茸毡必待表欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208808_comment'></div>政和元年辛丑，嵩山晁说之谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1208808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　四月为天台僧作序。作品：《仁王护国般若经疏序》<div id='poem_1208783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仁王护国般若经疏序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208783")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208783'>陈隋间，天台智者远禀龙树立一大教，九传而至荆溪，荆溪复又九传而至新罗法融，传理应，理应传瑛纯，皆新罗人，以故此教播于日本而海外盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208783_comment'></div>属中原丧乱，典籍荡灭，虽此教是为不可亡者，亦难乎其存也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208783_comment'></div>然杲日将出而晓霞先升，真人应运而文明自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208783_comment'></div>我有宋之初，此教乃渐航海入吴越，今世所传三大部之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208783_comment'></div>然尚有留而不至，与夫至而非其本真者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208783_comment'></div>《仁王经疏》先至有二本，众咸斥其伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208783_comment'></div>昔法智既纳日本信禅师所寄辟支佛发，答其所问二十义，乃求其所谓《仁王经疏》，信即授诸海舶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208783_comment'></div>无何，中流大风惊涛，舶人念无以息龙鼍之怒，遽投斯疏以慰安之，法智乃求强记者二僧诣信，使读诵以归，而二僧死于日本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208783_comment'></div>至元丰初，海贾乃持今《仁王经疏》三卷来四明，于是老僧如恂因缘得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208783_comment'></div>其文显而旨微，言约而意广，以秦译为本，义势似《观心论疏》，实章安所记智者之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208783_comment'></div>恂道孤而寡偶，学古而难知，食贫而力不足，无以为此经毫发之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208783_comment'></div>每指而叹曰：「其来晚而艰如此，宁封野马而饱蠹鱼，不能下几案以视人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208783_comment'></div>呜呼，此疏曾不得辈行于三大部中，而匿光瘗彩，犹若海外之远欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208783_comment'></div>恂今年七十有六岁，乃一日抱之而泣曰：「殆将与吾俱灭耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208783_comment'></div>吾前日之志非也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208783_comment'></div>过嵩山晁说之曰：「曷不为我序而流通之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208783_comment'></div>说之自顾何足以与此，亦尝有言曰：智者若生齐梁之前，则达磨不复西来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208783_comment'></div>尽法性为止观，而源流释迦之道，囊橐达磨之旨，今方盛于越中，异日会当周于天下，岂独是书之不可掩哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208783_comment'></div>顾予老不及见之为恨，姑序其所自云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208783_comment'></div>政和二年壬辰四月癸卯，朝请郎、飞骑尉、赐绯鱼袋晁说之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1208783_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　五月作序，拟西归。作品：《不二门指归序》<div id='poem_1208784' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208784' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208784?labeling=true' target='_blank'>不二门指归叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208784")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208784_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208784'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208784'>天台之教著明于法智，而法智晚出高弟曰南屏臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208784_comment'></div>臻在熙宁中尚无恙，予时随侍杭州，与群儿辈游南屏，而不知有臻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208784_comment'></div>逮今将四十年，白发飘零，宦游明州，遇臻之高弟如恂，始知有臻，而恨前日未尝游南屏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208784_comment'></div>年少不知好，而老大自伤者，可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208784_comment'></div>恂今年七十有六岁矣，志刚而气明，议论慷慨，不少下人，特推功于其师，每喜道其当时从学艰勤之状，且不讳其诃斥诲责之语，得非所志者笃，而所得者深欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208784_comment'></div>臻之善固使人不能忘，愈久而益亲耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208784_comment'></div>今予将西去，恂乃出南屏门人所记《不二门指归》一篇曰：「久不以视人，宜为序以布露之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208784_comment'></div>序虽不足与知，颇喜臻得名既高，而兹又有以副其名，慰后生之望，予亦恍然如前日与臻接而不复恨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208784_comment'></div>因念四方游客临浙江、至南屏者不乏人，而能知臻者几何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208784_comment'></div>实待此书发之欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208784_comment'></div>彼为天台之学者，尚何言耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208784_comment'></div>辄书其所感而序之云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208784_comment'></div>政和二年壬辰五月癸亥，嵩山晁说之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1208784_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在明州曾病目多日。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在明州，与丛林往还。作品：《还琦公诗卷》《次韵和法琦》《辩字赠恂公》《惧说赠然公》<div id='poem_197423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送琦公诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197423")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197423'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197423'>孤山教体外，赋诗汤休上。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197423'>后来数参寥，接手得宗匠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197423'>东游四明山，怀人增恻怆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197423'>何言遇老琦，二公论辈行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197423'>但欠主盟人，汲古自清唱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197423'>明年已七十<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作旬）</span>，句法何荡漾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197423'>兹山近蓬莱，展卷到绝旷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197423'>岛子敢赓酬，我正恨难傍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197423'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_197423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197423'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_197423_0'>⑴ 自注：明人称村夫为岛子（原缺，据四库本补）。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197423_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_197383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和法琦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197383")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197383'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197383'>野寺木鱼午不响，老僧乞米樵松根。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197383'>志幽思苦作诗戏，处身不忌如洼樽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197383'>大轴视我正其欲，尚恨近体意虚辱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197383'>报以五字陶谢家，要看素丝难纯束。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197383'>江头梅雨灭槐火，我正思公惭饭颗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197383'>复我<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作哦）</span>苦淡来恼予，叹息有能无不可。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197383'>枉是昼公出前溪，猥效苏州失故栖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197383'>苏州风流今不见，公乎老矣谁提携。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197383'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_197383_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208976?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辩字赠恂公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208976")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208976'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208976'>老僧如恂来，为予言天台智者之教，曰：「介尔有心，即具三十」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208976_comment'></div>予问：「何谓介尔」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208976_comment'></div>曰：「自吾祖荆溪以来，皆以《诗》『介尔景福』为證」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208976_comment'></div>予按诗家训介曰助也，与智者之意了不相当，奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208976_comment'></div>颇闻荆溪无不该洽，而于此一字似或误矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208976_comment'></div>虽然，不害其为荆溪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208976_comment'></div>此字盖当如《汉书》「介居河北」之介，晋灼曰：「介，时也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208976_comment'></div>讫点反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208976_comment'></div>夫此有心一适当其时，霍然之顷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208976_comment'></div>又如《素问》所谓「心欬之状，喉中介介如梗」，读亦如戛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208976_comment'></div>夫介介之梗，可以见彼「介尔有心」之相欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208976_comment'></div>又《易》「介于石」，古文作砎，郑康成云「磨砎也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208976_comment'></div>古八反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208976_comment'></div>夫磨砎之声，亦倏然而有者也，读者可以意了，而见智者之语峻意洁云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208976_comment'></div>恂曰：「窃尝有意而不知其读如此，愿书之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208976_comment'></div>予每恨晚辈辄废形声之学，喜书以赠恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208976_comment'></div>政和元年辛卯十一月己卯，嵩山景迂生书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1208976_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惧说赠然公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208977")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208977'>予尝怪韩文公、欧阳文忠公力排浮图，而其门多浮图之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208977_comment'></div>如澄观、契嵩辈，虽自能传于后世，而士大夫今喜称道之者，实二公之力为多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208977_comment'></div>夫毁其教而进其徒，岂非一反哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208977_comment'></div>往年孤山智圆凛然有名当世，自成一家之学，而读书甚博，性晓文章经纬，师法韩文公，常责其学者不如韩能有功于孔氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208977_comment'></div>近则嵩力辩欧阳之谤，有古义士之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208977_comment'></div>是二人者，忘其雠而慕其善，又一反哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208977_comment'></div>窃尝思之，是惟公乎好恶而务乎厚，不自窘束而坛宇广大者，为能如此，若其反乃其合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208977_comment'></div>天台僧了然字焕之，年三十六岁，天姿秀发，传其教甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208977_comment'></div>比尝辛苦于山中十有五年，众服其善，而自觉其有得，乃出游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208977_comment'></div>予始识于四明，而叹异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208977_comment'></div>顾予方流落不为人所比数，尚何有于斯人，而窃为之惧则深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208977_comment'></div>盖斯人贤可妒而能可嫉，余于彼妒嫉者则无所恨，而唯惧斯人聚徒太早，又惧其著书不能待晚而太锐，封植师说疆界抵太牢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208977_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208977_comment'></div>今有人视其外所师说者，不怨则怒，或阳善而阴伐之，其如师说不能一字不谬，何得非嗜聋好瞽而与之共毙欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208977_comment'></div>世间书读固不能尽，而应有当有者又如晨炊之不可缓，何容年少辄有著述？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208977_comment'></div>锐气喜瑕痹先达，不知己之所谓新者，过少时又复陈腐，有人议之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208977_comment'></div>以故少年著书者至晚必悔，如其不悔者，又无足观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208977_comment'></div>然之祖智者犹以领徒早为厉己，况他人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208977_comment'></div>然宜勉斯三者，公其好恶而务乎厚，不自窘束而坛宇广大，则善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208977_comment'></div>不过数年，予当隐处嵩山，或闻东南有道盛行，大得名誉者，是必然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208977_comment'></div>然其勉诸，作《惧说》赠之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1208977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1113')">1112-1113年</a>　在明州。作品：《闻四明人不喜秋千因作》《戏作》《秋日有感因诵王元之……》《偶见司马公休陈无几书简感旧作绝句》《年年至日常为客》《咋舌》《春初》《寄昭德兄弟》《大热戏作》《忆江南赠通叟年兄》《偶见陈诚之一诗……》《依韵和蔡天启》《与吕舜徒书》《答陈秀才书》《答朱子云书》《答池州邓君书》<div id='poem_196908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻四明人不喜鞦韆因作</a><span id='poem_sentence_5_197336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197336'>饥肠虽自鸣，寒冻非吾事。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197336_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
