href='/Writing/197350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆江南赠通叟年兄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197350")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197350'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197350'>北客而南征，蹇产非所志。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197350'>问津人尚绝，后来狂避世。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197350'>流离窜斥者，其数非一二。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197350'>风流称南朝，文物始佳丽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197350'>要途在荆扬，僻左处吴会。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197350'>吴会兴国来，乃以丹漆贵。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197350'>若其大才豪，终是江南最。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197350'>君家住江南，豫章生次第。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197350'>非但吾言逼，正尔百忧似。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197350'>易见岩下电，难识斗间气。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197350'>结绶三十年，胆<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作挟）</span>策未一试。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197350'>譬如瑚与琏，讵落日中市。<div id='poem_sentence_11_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_197350'>飘然渡浙江，式慰此憔悴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_197350'>我屋梁园久，近卜嵩峰邃。<div id='poem_sentence_13_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_197350'>海虫难下箸，粟浆有贱嗜。<div id='poem_sentence_14_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_197350'>不读非圣书，忍更增疣赘。<div id='poem_sentence_15_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_197350'>又不求甚解，未肯争破碎。<div id='poem_sentence_16_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_197350'>排闷亦吟哦，清潦谁滋味。<div id='poem_sentence_17_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_197350'>自从住囚<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作注罪）</span>籍，一语不敢谓。<div id='poem_sentence_18_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_197350'>岂惟要绝言，自憎生此喙。<div id='poem_sentence_19_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_197350'>因君发吾狂，明当保严誓。<div id='poem_sentence_20_197350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_197350'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_197350_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶见陈诚之一诗不胜钦叹辄纪赠求其巨篇深愧芜累</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197525")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197525'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197525'>四明唐中叶，处士有陈深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197525'>书既殚万象，诗想瑶华音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197525'>惜哉不并传，裔孙自苦吟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197525'>岂易识此孙，海底珊瑚沉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197525'>邂逅我见之，昔恨阻冲襟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197525'>念我理归棹，旅梦断遥岑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197525'>愿乞十九首，降尽河外心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197525'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_197525_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吕舜徒书<span class='inlineComment2'>（明州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208754")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208754'>说之启：去年十二月二十五日，鄞县递中为问，达否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208754_comment'></div>昨日忽收十一月二十七日书，承侍奉万福，至慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208754_comment'></div>说之远宦，穷寂如初，无足言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208754_comment'></div>贯弟得从贤者游，尤可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208754_comment'></div>所谓「乐有贤父兄」之说，则未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208754_comment'></div>是出于《孟子》乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208754_comment'></div>试为吾友陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208754_comment'></div>乐贤而恶不才，在敌以上有所不行，况吾父兄之间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208754_comment'></div>父兄天性，甘勉其孝悌而不能已，宁知所乐贤不贤耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208754_comment'></div>贤可乐矣，顾不贤则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208754_comment'></div>且如何而可谓之贤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208754_comment'></div>颜氏之子、闵氏之弟，视孔鲤不免有惭色矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208754_comment'></div>舜五十而慕，为瞽叟之贤欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208754_comment'></div>文王问王季安否而忧喜，王季之德不与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208754_comment'></div>孔子亦曰：「喜父母之年耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208754_comment'></div>以此三圣人之迹求之，似孟子之言无所当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208754_comment'></div>且其言父子之间不责善，则疏之矣，今何望之深耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208754_comment'></div>七丈讲学最明，侍次以此禀之，便可语诸郎曰：「无以吾不贤而恶之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208754_comment'></div>此语虽近乎戏，然所感不浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208754_comment'></div>近作《申刘》一篇，辨舜河南事，辄同往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208754_comment'></div>汪信民乃止于此，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208754_comment'></div>令人痛怛不可言，吾党中失此一人，大有所系，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208754_comment'></div>颇恨信民不及见吾《申刘》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208754_comment'></div>诸郎各想进学，春寒，万万为亲多爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208754_comment'></div>递中奉状，草草不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208754_comment'></div>正月二十六日，说之上舜徒船场朝奉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1208754_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208758?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈秀才书<span class='inlineComment2'>（明州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208758")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208758_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208758'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208758'>说之启，陈君秀才足下：比蒙见临，昨日又辱长书，仰叹文旨甚高，非所宜施也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208758_comment'></div>说之驽下，虽少得师友而无成，老矣，所尚者不过先儒传注之说，其有甚不得已，而必当改易者，低徊顾瞻，宁失之怯，而不敢过乎勇，又何敢借申韩以为奇险，而攘释老以增高远哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208758_comment'></div>大要是知蛇本无足耳，身被俗学之名而甘之，何所逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208758_comment'></div>足下乃独谓之古学，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208758_comment'></div>去吾嵩颍，乘兴宦游江湖数千里之外，往往指其衣巾而笑之，又性率不自昧，辄辩南北之学，虽途人而怒目怀雠者有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208758_comment'></div>足下复尔称誉之，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208758_comment'></div>人之嗜好，盐梅不同，一至此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208758_comment'></div>夫子既没，洙泗之上，并汾之间，孰有如曾子、子思有功于斯文者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208758_comment'></div>世乃略而不道，似古人无曾、孔、荀、孟之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208758_comment'></div>在本朝则柳仲涂、张晦之、穆伯长、贾公疏诸公皆尊孔氏，以振我国家礼乐文明之风者，奈何后生漫不知其姓名，则目前碌碌尚何为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208758_comment'></div>足下所责于不肖者，抑又何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208758_comment'></div>无或贻足下之悔乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208758_comment'></div>政此多雨，江步艰难，未及往谒，先此布意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208758_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208758_comment'></div>十月二十三日，嵩山晁说之上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1208758_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答朱子云书<span class='inlineComment2'>（明州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208760")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208760'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208760'>说之启：辱问荷意甚厚，且叹足下不忧樵苏而惟汲汲斯文也，甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208760_comment'></div>所是性与天道不可闻者，不谓亦出于足下之口也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208760_comment'></div>今之学者大抵巧慧于古人之言，而斲丧其意，莫斯为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208760_comment'></div>子贡抑扬叹息其所闻之语，便谓之真无所闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208760_comment'></div>譬如学古文者，恨《九歌》、《九章》难及，彼方为时文者未尝对《离骚》面，宁论其难不难耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208760_comment'></div>《论语》此类不少，寻常相见，无因发之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208760_comment'></div>至于学《易》尤不可遽，说之从弟冲之颇有才思，临出京师，欲来传《易》，告之云：「吾弟初未尝为小王《易》，尚未可言京氏《易》，况于商瞿、子木之学耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208760_comment'></div>请以三年为期，老兄归自四明，吾弟熟乎王氏、京氏之浅深，然后及之未晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208760_comment'></div>譬如不由门庭而巧入堂奥，深则深矣，其如门外之事何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208760_comment'></div>古之学者岂不有次第哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208760_comment'></div>亦敢以此为足下谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208760_comment'></div>顷年尝作《易规》十一篇，今以往，足下试一读之，以谓如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208760_comment'></div>馀迟面言，不一一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208760_comment'></div>六日，说之上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1208760_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答池州邓君书<span class='inlineComment2'>（明州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208759")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208759'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208759'>说之启，邓君先辈大孝：前岁令兄司理来求公墓志，说之以令兄同郡守官之故，不得而辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208759_comment'></div>窃怪令兄初脱场屋事业，便好古文，求索于人而下及于仆，既而有以信之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208759_comment'></div>至于足下昧平生于千馀里之外，无或以仆之文为怪异不祥之物欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208759_comment'></div>忽人来惠书，开喻勤至，又复释然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208759_comment'></div>足下方此不文时，言词亹亹，驰骋下上，孝思之所感欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208759_comment'></div>抑其平昔注意不凡邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208759_comment'></div>甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208759_comment'></div>更冀日祭读礼经之馀，悉取古人书读之，师友先儒，无望专一经以成人之理，如五䌽不具而能绘事，自结绳既代之后无此理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208759_comment'></div>足下以此光扬先烈，于仆何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208759_comment'></div>因思仆少时所作文，全未有次第，不知当是何敢效于一二宗匠前，而彼一二宗匠又何遽推奖荐闻之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208759_comment'></div>逮今日白首，粗能杼柚分经纬，而无一人相知者，前辈先九泉，可胜言耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208759_comment'></div>不意足下今日顾我良为不浅，他时或得相见悉此怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208759_comment'></div>未间，更希节哀多爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208759_comment'></div>人遽回，适病目多日，不及详尽，仍不果亲书，并幸恕察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208759_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208759_comment'></div>月日，说之上。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1208759'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1208759_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

郑州

-----title
富县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c0d57a182b0a4669b0ecffdefa2b1e79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c0d57a182b0a4669b0ecffdefa2b1e79");'><span id='c0d57a182b0a4669b0ecffdefa2b1e79_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　秋后赴任鄜州通判。作品：《河中戏作绝句》《跋米元章与赵景升帖》《缺门还王三兄师文》《河中府古兴寄刘壮舆》《至河中首访鬼拔河图……》《赴鄜州京郑间途中作》《河中府追怀王二兄及思永兴十二弟》《初至鄜州感事》<div id='poem_196870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河中戏作绝句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_196870")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196870'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196870'>人物英雄异姓王，山河生气尚光芒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196870_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196870'>可怜只解誇佳丽，花落春空更断肠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196870_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196870'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196870_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋米元章与赵景升帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208810")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208810'>通州防御使令晙既窆孝恭公之志铭，雪泪而言曰：「卜日有期，因使刻画未工，播传且不远广，二恨没身，将无以赎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208810_comment'></div>乃移诸横石，增笔墨之美，而施则无穷，君子于是知孝恭之所以为孝恭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208810_comment'></div>既自躬之，复见其子之源流，可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208810_comment'></div>伏念燕懿王体貌魁伟，谨慎寡言，好读书，无犬马之玩，是孝恭之所自邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208810_comment'></div>政和四年甲午六月戊午，嵩山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1208810_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缺门遇王三兄师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197517")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197517'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197517'>生民本羁旅，何以娱今朝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197517'>风雨崤渑道，离别秋冬交。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197517'>忽复有好怀，故人道旁招。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197517'>如狂语错乱，疑梦情飘飘<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作摇）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197517'>君须<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作发）</span>何尽白，我志则全消。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197517'>忧患君恐可，图书兴尚豪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197517'>玷圭宜委土，良骥乃系匏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197517'>但愿不再辱，敢慕无久劳<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：师文欲乞宫观。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197517'>马蹄分异县，朔吹结同袍。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197517'>三年以为期，嵩少理居巢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197517'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_197517_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河中府古兴寄刘杜舆</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197450")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197450'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197450'>肘腋患难御，垣墙倾莫制。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197450'>兹者<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作遐哉）</span>论战国，破秦必在魏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197450'>初疑此语谩，身到识真是。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197450'>河山既设险，信食以自治。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197450'>秦虽百虎狼，得进不得退。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197450'>襄王昧远图，苏秦嗜近利。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197450'>惜哉计画疏，为此山河愧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197450'>我怀谁与语，刘子长论议。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197450'>方为十二史，吾言不可废。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197450'>眺听常思君，梦魂先朔吹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197450'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_197450_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至河中首访鬼拔河图有画人云因陆学士移其壁乃<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>毁寸尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作许）</span>令人感慨终日有作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197390")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197390_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_197390_0'>① 原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197390'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197390'>坎坎分明拔河戏，盛在北朝唐尚尔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197390'>画手何人郑子虔，妙不戏人惟戏鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197390'>更无狞厉可严怖，既曰依人人是拟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197390'>家家贾勇负胜馀，见之心宁不知耻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197390'>最是隋宫窈窕春，汗妆蓬发羞相比。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197390'>故宜落笔在蒲州，门外河来三万里。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197390'>邻几舍人有拓本，诗翁赋诗名更起。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197390'>咏诗想画二十年，客舍此邦心自喜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197390'>揽真永绝伪物欺，顾影岂尽形仪美。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197390'>嗟予断绝百事心，痴处留情独在此。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197390'>魑魅魍魉好奔迸，文彩风流终弃圮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197390'>出门访之无处所，惜哉史君陆子履。<div id='poem_sentence_11_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_197390'>但欲便坐易瞻玩，不知壁古难移徙。<div id='poem_sentence_12_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_197390'>岂无剥落一寸馀，我愿宝之若琼蕊。<div id='poem_sentence_13_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_197390'>不然当学补亡诗，收拾粉本细纲纪。<div id='poem_sentence_14_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_197390'>或谓前年九鼎成，时无杂糅清如水。<div id='poem_sentence_15_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_197390'>虽有高室谁瞰之，亦莫揶揄毛手指。<div id='poem_sentence_16_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_197390'>帖壁不祥宜遁逃，䌽门抛捘方靡靡。<div id='poem_sentence_17_197390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_197390'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_197390_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_515831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_515831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/515831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴鄜州京郑间途中作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_515831")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_515831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_515831'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_515831'>园林叶落丹丘远，坂路霜寒白发侵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_515831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_515831'>不是关西将家子，也无诗思著秦音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_515831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_515831'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_515831_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197174' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197174' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197174?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河中府追怀亡二兄及思永兴十二弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197174")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197174_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197174'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197174'>表里山河季布州，我家兄弟忆同游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197174'>芸香寂寞空青冢<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：二兄学士尝守此郡。）</span>，绛帐飘零欲白头<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：十二弟为此郡教授。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197174'>羁旅即今无好语，登临自古有高楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197174'>颇闻酬唱西岩在，阙里诸孙添我愁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197174'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197174'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_197174_0'>⑴ 自注：兄弟在此郡时，孔毅甫提点刑狱，多唱和。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197174_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_197401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初至鄜州感事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197401")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197401'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197401'>罪斥云一纪，常亦守官箴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197401'>置身江海畔，放言麋鹿岑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197401'>大吏不呵谴，小吏自堪任。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197401'>虾菜日异馔，著书敌南金。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197401'>岂无二三子，善叩响不沈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197401'>更逢四高士<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：杲、恂、立、然。）</span>，语妙何愔愔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197401'>俯揽尘土影，仰摅冰玉心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197401'>苦辛虽在昔，菑穫实于今。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197401'>归榜不忍速，故庐尚可寻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197401'>金闺朝轇轕，荃壁<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作兰）</span>梦萧森。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197401'>领阔贻尔诮，新贵使我瘖。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197401'>饥寒一丈室<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去年京师大雪。）</span>，奔走九秋砧<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_197401'>长坂马难健，败絮虱易侵。<div id='poem_sentence_12_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_197401'>池西别故旧，税驾雕山阴。<div id='poem_sentence_13_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_197401'>白翟无曩迹，赫连有脱镡。<div id='poem_sentence_14_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_197401'>幸哉廊庙术，勇不誇纵<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作众）</span>擒。<div id='poem_sentence_15_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_197401'>誓表前日来，父子恩更深。<div id='poem_sentence_16_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_197401'>战士老腐粟，癯儒适懦襟。<div id='poem_sentence_17_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_197401'>羊肥卧沙种，酒美西凉斟。<div id='poem_sentence_18_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_197401'>农武自先烈，五律勤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>窥临<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_197401'>礼乐被远俗，三叹斥哇淫<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：予按外邑新乐。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_20_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_197401'>勉旃不再辱，聊尔容华簪。<div id='poem_sentence_21_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_197401'>敛迹有馀愧，难闻弦诵音<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_22_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_197401'>尚喜屋山阿，双泉如鸣琴。<div id='poem_sentence_23_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_197401'>远明桑苧翁，品茶疑未谌。<div id='poem_sentence_24_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_197401'>洞中有仙者，得度人骎骎。<div id='poem_sentence_25_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_197401'>长生非敢望，却粒实所钦。<div id='poem_sentence_26_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_197401'>肠空不贮愁，虑绝发奇祲。<div id='poem_sentence_27_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_197401'>何劳东皋计，即日返幽林。<div id='poem_sentence_28_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_197401'>难忘平昔兴，一为梁甫吟。<div id='poem_sentence_29_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_197401'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_197401_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197401'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_197401_0'>⑴ 自注：今秋数往来郑、蔡，遂为西行。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_197401_0'>⑵ 原作勒，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_197401_1'>⑶ 自注：予专察视保甲，今年初教五阵。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_22_197401_0'>⑷ 自注：予以名在邪籍，不得干与学事。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197401_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在鄜州任上。作品：《记京房易传后》《刘氏藏书记》<div id='poem_1208801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记京房易传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208801")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208801'>《汉艺文志》：《易》，京氏凡三种八十九篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208801_comment'></div>《隋·经籍志》有京《章句》十卷，又有占候十种七十三卷，《唐艺文志》有京《章句》十卷，而占候存者五种二十三卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208801_comment'></div>今其《章句》亡矣，乃略见于僧一行及李鼎祚之书，而其传者曰《易传》三卷，《积算杂占条例法》一卷，或共题《易传》四卷，而名皆与古不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208801_comment'></div>今所谓《京氏易传》者或题曰《京氏积算易传》，疑《隋》、《唐志》之《错卦》是也，《错卦》在隋七卷，唐八卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208801_comment'></div>所谓《积算杂占条例法》者，疑隋《逆刺占灾异》十二卷是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208801_comment'></div>至唐《逆刺》三卷，而亡其九卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208801_comment'></div>元祐八年高丽进书，有《京氏周易占》十卷，疑《隋志》《周易占》十二卷是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208801_comment'></div>自古《易》家有书而无师者多矣，京氏之书幸而与存者，才十之一，尚何谁之师哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208801_comment'></div>说之自元丰壬戌偶脱去举子事业，便有意学《易》，而辄不好王氏，妄以谓弼之外当自有名家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208801_comment'></div>果得《京氏传》，而文字颠倒舛讹，不可训知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208801_comment'></div>逮其服习既久，渐有所窥，今三十有四年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208801_comment'></div>乃能以其象数辨正文字之谬于边郡山房寂寞之中，而私识之曰：是书兆乾坤之二象，以成八卦，卦凡八变而六十有四，于其往来升降之际，以观消息盈虚于天地之元，而酬酢乎万物之表者，炳然在目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208801_comment'></div>大抵辨三易，运五行，正四时，谨二十四气，悉七十二候，而位五星，降二十八宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208801_comment'></div>其进退以几而为一卦之主者，谓之「世」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208801_comment'></div>奇偶相与，据一以超二，而为主之相者，谓之「应」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208801_comment'></div>世之所位而阴阳肇乎所配<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，而终不脱乎本<span class='inlineComment2'>（以飞某卦之位，乃伏某宫之位。）</span>，以隐赜佐神明者，谓之「伏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208801_comment'></div>起乎世而合内外，参乎本数以纪月者谓之「建」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208801_comment'></div>终终始始极乎数而不可穷以纪日者，谓之「积」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208801_comment'></div>含于中而以四为用，一卦备四卦者，谓之「互」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208801_comment'></div>乾建甲子于初，坤建甲午于上，八卦之上乃生一世之初，一世之五位乃分而为五世之位，其五世之上乃为游魂之世，五世之初乃为归魂之世，而归魂之初乃生后卦之初，其建刚日则节气，柔日则中气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208801_comment'></div>其数虚则二十有八，盈则三十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208801_comment'></div>盖其可言者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208801_comment'></div>若夫象遗乎意，意遗乎言，则错总其用，唯变所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208801_comment'></div>或两相配而论内外二象，若世与内<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，若世与外<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，或不论内外二象而论其内外之位<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>，或三相参而论内外与飞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>，若伏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>，或相参而论内外世应建伏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>，不论内外而论世建与飞伏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>，或兼论世应飞伏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑼</sup>，或专论世应<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑽</sup>，或论世之所忌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑾</sup>，或论世之所生<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑿</sup>，于其所起见其所灭<span class='inlineComment2'>（《大壮》起于子，灭于亥。）</span>，于其所刑见其所生<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒀</sup>，故曰死于位，生于时，死于时，生于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_comment'></div>苟非彰往而察来，微显而阐幽者，曷足以与此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208801_comment'></div>前是焦小黄变四千九十有六卦，后有管辂定《乾》之轨七百六十有八，《坤》之轨六百七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208801_comment'></div>其知之者将可以语邵康节之《易》矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208801_comment'></div>彼小王之徒，唯知尚其辞耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208801_comment'></div>其谓斯何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208801_comment'></div>昔鲁商瞿子木受《易》孔子，五传而至汉田何子装，何授洛阳丁宽，宽授砀田王孙，王孙授东海孟喜，喜授梁焦赣延寿，延寿授房，房授东海殷嘉、河东姚平、河南乘弘、繇是《易》有京氏之学而传盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208801_comment'></div>有瞿牧白生者，不肯京氏，曰：「京非孟氏学也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208801_comment'></div>刘向亦疑京托之孟氏，予不知当时为何说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208801_comment'></div>今以当时之书验之，盖有孟氏、京房十一篇，灾异孟氏、京房六十六篇，与夫京氏、殷嘉十二篇，同为一家之学，则其源委孰可诬哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208801_comment'></div>此亦学者不可不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208801_comment'></div>若小王者，果何所授受邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208801_comment'></div>盖自京氏为王学有馀力，而王学之适京氏则无繇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208801_comment'></div>或传是书而文字舛谬，得以予言而考诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208801_comment'></div>今有不可就正者，阙以待来哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208801_comment'></div>《积算杂占条例法》具如别录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208801_comment'></div>政和五年乙未五月庚辰，嵩山晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1208801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1208801'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1208801_0'>⑴ 《乾》与《坤》、《震》与《巽》、《坎》与《离》、《艮》与《兑》。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑵ 《革》水火配位，内《离》火四世水。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑶ 《困》金木交争，外《兑》金初世木。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑷ 《萃》土水入《艮》、《兑》，初土四水。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑸ 《贲》土火木分阴阳，《艮》土《离》火飞木。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑹ 《旅》火土木入《离》《艮》，《离》火《艮》土伏木。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑺ 《观》金土火木互为体，建金世，应内土，伏火外木。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑻ 《益》金土入《震》《巽》，世与飞土，建与伏金。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑼ 《复》水土见候，世应水土，飞伏水土；《屯》土木应象，世应土木，飞伏土木。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑽ 《夬》金木合乾兑，入坤象，世金应木；《蛊》金木入艮巽，世金应木。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑾ 《履》金火入卦，初九火、九四火克九五世金及乾之金。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⑿ 《巽》火木与巽同宫，世水巽木建火。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1208801_0'>⒀ 《随》金木交刑，水火相激，《兑》金《巽》木。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1208801_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1208998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘氏藏书记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年7月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208998")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208998'>汉承秦焚书灭学之后，赖故老口所诵，数得闻先王之遗训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208998_comment'></div>厥后广开献书之路，至武帝时外有太常、太史、博士之藏，内有延阁、广内、秘室之府，虽盛矣，然至成帝时乃大备著录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208998_comment'></div>盖约法天下不出一日之中，而藏书掌固必待百年之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208998_comment'></div>隋御府书所以特号称最盛者，以其平一南北，而坐兼南北朝之所有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208998_comment'></div>夫县官之势何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208998_comment'></div>独于藏书一事，其勤如此，况在学士大夫之家邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208998_comment'></div>刘歆自称三代之书蕴崇于家，直不计尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208998_comment'></div>盖自楚元王而来，世尚文雅，而护都水使者又复博极群书，无不充足，而歆因得以誇邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208998_comment'></div>昔人谓三代仕宦而衣，五代仕宦而食，不知书又在衣食之上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208998_comment'></div>都官刘公凝之卓行绝识，不待老而归休庐山之下，其遗子孙者无他物，盖唯图书而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208998_comment'></div>其子道原少而日诵万言，既长苦心笃志，无所嗜好，昼夜以读书为娱，至于不慕荣利，忘去寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208998_comment'></div>司马温公称其精博，宋次道称其该赡，范醇夫称其密致，则其所藏复蕴崇而不计者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208998_comment'></div>且尝愤疾南方士人家不藏书矣，则于是盖特加意焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208998_comment'></div>公之子羲仲壮舆，人视其迈往不群，而自处惮惮循约，唯恐前修之辱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208998_comment'></div>从仕四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208998_comment'></div>妻子不免饥寒，而敦然唯是之求索，甚于人之饥渴而赴饮食者，则其所得不特补其家之未足，而且有以振发国中之沈郁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208998_comment'></div>既已踵成其父《十国纪年》，而身采周秦之遗文以为《十二国史》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208998_comment'></div>尝论著《春秋》矣，而方且为《周易》之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208998_comment'></div>则其藏书岂特充牣箧笥而誇缃帙，如愚贾润屋以金珠邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208998_comment'></div>于是谨识其所得书之岁月先后，以视子孙，其意为不浅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208998_comment'></div>乃俾说之为之记，以载于目录之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208998_comment'></div>昔之时，如任昉、沈约辈，号为藏书之家者，今不复论，而论诸本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208998_comment'></div>如王文康初于周相世宗，多有唐室旧书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208998_comment'></div>今其子孙不知何在，宁论其书之存亡，而所有者书目一编，使好事者对之兴叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208998_comment'></div>李文贞所藏既富，而且辟学馆以延学士大夫，不待见主人，而下马直入读书，供牢饩以给其日力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208998_comment'></div>与众共利之如此，宜其书永久而不复零落；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208998_comment'></div>今其家仅有败屋数楹，而书不知何在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208998_comment'></div>凡名公卿大夫、儒林之士所有之书，往往随其人而逝矣，传诸再世者盖寡，而况曾玄之守邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208998_comment'></div>惟是宋宣献家四世以名德相继，而兼有毕丞相、杨文庄二家之书，其富盖有王府不及者，元符中一夕灾为灰烬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208998_comment'></div>予家则五世于兹也，虽不敢与宋氏争多，而校雠是正则未肯自让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208998_comment'></div>乃去年冬火亦告谴，不谓前日悲怆痛恨乎宋氏者，今自涕泣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208998_comment'></div>呜呼，其不艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208998_comment'></div>壮舆家于庐山之阳，宽闲之野，不复有京师火灾之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208998_comment'></div>上方兴礼乐，议封禅，则又永不顾盗贼兵甲之祸，而刘氏之书与七泽俱富矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208998_comment'></div>后之人视予言而祗敬先德，不忘前日畜积之艰而勉强学行，则为书之荣也大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208998_comment'></div>其书凡若干卷云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208998_comment'></div>政和乙未七月十一日戊寅，嵩山晁说之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1208998_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年7月22日</a>　在鄜州任上，校《中庸传》，改正错简。<div id='poem_1208879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中庸传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年7月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208879")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208879'>○○●「天命之谓性」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208879_comment'></div>性者中之所寓也，莫知其所自而推言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1208879'>「率性之谓道者」何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208879_comment'></div>性得所率则为君子，不得其所率则为小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208879_comment'></div>曰诚、曰明、曰孝、曰忠、曰恕、曰和，皆率性之具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208879_comment'></div>是六者，皆中之所以为中者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1208879'>「修道之谓教者」何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208879_comment'></div>圣人所以经纶天下之大经也，君子所以择乎中庸也，小人所以反乎中庸者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1208879'>●「道也者，不可须臾离也，可离非道也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208879_comment'></div>出乎性而教之所本也，君子以是诚之务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1208879'>●「是故君子戒慎乎其所不睹，恐惧乎其所不闻」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208879_comment'></div>中也，诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1208879'>●「莫见乎隐，莫显乎微，故君子慎其独也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208879_comment'></div>中也，明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1208879'>○●「喜怒哀乐之未发谓之中」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208879_comment'></div>情之未发，性之全纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208879_comment'></div>中之所以名中者也，肫肫如也，渊渊如也，浩浩如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1208879'>「发而皆中节谓之和」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208879_comment'></div>中之一物，于是乎有二名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208879_comment'></div>颠沛之际，毫发之多，或不中节焉，亦不足为和也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208879_comment'></div>有子言和，必有待乎节之非，和之正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1208879'>「中也者，天下之大本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208879_comment'></div>和也者，天下之达道也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208879_comment'></div>是一物不得二名也，楩楠豫章之大本，而不达道则亦恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1208879'>「致中和，天地位焉，万物育焉」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208879_comment'></div>教之行也，明道先生，常善乎致之言也，常善乎位之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1208879'>○○●「仲尼曰：君子中庸，小人反中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208879_comment'></div>君子之中庸也，君子而时中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208879_comment'></div>小人之中庸也，小人而无忌惮也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208879_comment'></div>中之所以为常道也，君子而时中，则无时而不中也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208879_comment'></div>小人而无忌惮，须臾变改，莫之能中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208879_comment'></div>以是知先儒说用中为常道是也，近世说中说庸，非所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208879_comment'></div>王肃本作小人之反中庸也，胡先生、温公、明道先生皆云然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208879_comment'></div>问者曰：「庸得非变邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208879_comment'></div>所以济中者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208879_comment'></div>曰：是不识中者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208879_comment'></div>君子之中随所器而丽焉，不动而变，尚何所假也邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208879_comment'></div>子莫执中无权者，是子莫知中非君子之中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208879_comment'></div>刘侍读曰：「中庸者，中用也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208879_comment'></div>盖亦误也，言中斯用之也，先儒曰用中为常道是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208879_comment'></div>刘说前见于皇氏、熊氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1208879'>○●「子曰：中庸其至矣乎，民鲜能久矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208879_comment'></div>教之不行也，有中庸之君，斯有中庸之民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1208879'>○●「子曰：道之不行也，我知之矣，知者过之，愚者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208879_comment'></div>道之不明也，我知之矣，贤者过之，不肖者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208879_comment'></div>人莫不饮食也，鲜能知味也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208879_comment'></div>子曰：道其不行矣夫」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208879_comment'></div>不诚不明则不中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1208879'>○●「子曰：舜其大知也与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208879_comment'></div>舜好问而好察迩言，隐恶而扬善，执其两端用其中于民，其斯以为舜乎」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208879_comment'></div>舜之所以为舜者中庸也，明诚两尽而道教行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1208879'>○○●「子曰：人皆曰予知，驱而纳诸罟擭陷阱之中，而莫之知辟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208879_comment'></div>人皆曰予知，择乎中庸，而不能期月守也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208879_comment'></div>不明不诚则不中也，择也者依也，斯人自谓之知者，非知之明也，君子不以为知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208879_comment'></div>昔夫子言仁知详矣，曾子、子思虑后世或泛然失其旨，乃以仁为诚，知为明，其实一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1208879'>○●「子曰：回之为人也，择乎中庸，得一善，则拳拳服膺而弗失之矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208879_comment'></div>回所以为回者，中庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208879_comment'></div>诚明两尽而道教行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1208879'>○「子曰：天下国家可均也，爵禄可辞也，白刃可蹈也，中庸不可能也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208879_comment'></div>惟诚明以之也，诚自成而道自道也，非功名利害外以怵之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1208879'>○○●「子路问强，子曰：南方之强与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208879_comment'></div>北方之强与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208879_comment'></div>抑而强与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208879_comment'></div>宽柔以教，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/161/Comments/0")'>不报</span>无道，南方之强也，君子居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/164/Comments/0")'>衽金革</span>，死而不厌，北方之强也，而强者居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208879_comment'></div>故君子和而不流，强哉矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208879_comment'></div>中立而不倚，强哉矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208879_comment'></div>国有道，不变塞焉，强哉矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208879_comment'></div>国无道，至死不变，强哉矫」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208879_comment'></div>强疑其非中也，盖惟中为能强也者诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208879_comment'></div>曾子论孝曰：「仁者人此者也，义者宜此者也，强者强此者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208879_comment'></div>强既有南北之异，则责子路之所安以勉乎中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208879_comment'></div>夫所谓君子者，既和既中而诚明之守，安于治乱之世，勤而勉之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208879_comment'></div>国有道，君子或易仕而改其度，不变塞也，强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1208879'>○○●「子曰：<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/195/Comments/0")'>素隐行怪</span>，后世有述焉，吾弗为之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208879_comment'></div>君子遵道而行，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/199/Comments/0")'>半涂而废</span>，吾弗能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/200/Comments/0")'>已矣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208879_comment'></div>君子依乎中庸，遁世不见知而不悔，唯圣者能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208879_comment'></div>君子之道，费而隐」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1208879_comment'></div>不诚不明，君子之所不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1208879_comment'></div>君子之遁世，亦中庸之依而安焉，又复依乎圣人之中庸，则其隐者，吾道之佹也，非故以意向之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1208879_comment'></div>郑氏曰：「道不费则仕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1208879_comment'></div>费者佹也，违也，《缁衣》有曰：「口费而烦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1208879_comment'></div>费或为哱，或为悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1208879'>●「夫妇之愚，可以与知焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1208879_comment'></div>及其至也，虽圣人亦有所不知焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1208879_comment'></div>夫妇之不肖，可以能行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1208879_comment'></div>及其至也，虽圣人亦有所不能焉」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1208879_comment'></div>唯明之知，唯诚之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1208879'>●「天地之大也，人犹有所憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1208879_comment'></div>故君子语大，天下万能载焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1208879_comment'></div>语小，天下莫能破焉」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1208879_comment'></div>中也诚也，语夫天下莫能事之大，则其大者诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1208879_comment'></div>语夫天下莫能分之小，则其小者诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1208879_comment'></div>盖虽大而中也，其小亦中也，人谁有憾于予哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_1208879'>●「诗云：『鸢飞戾天，鱼跃在渊』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1208879_comment'></div>言其上下察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1208879_comment'></div>君子之道造端乎夫妇，及其至也，察乎天地」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1208879_comment'></div>中也明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_1208879'>○○●「子曰：道不远人，人之为道而远人，不可以为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1208879_comment'></div>诗云：『伐柯伐柯，其则不远』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1208879_comment'></div>执柯以伐柯，睨而视之，犹以为远，故君子以人治人，改而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1208879_comment'></div>忠恕违道不远，施诸己而不愿，亦勿施于人」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1208879_comment'></div>忠恕之为中也，均率是性，而为道莫之或远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1208879_comment'></div>远于人则可须臾离也，以其不远人，而忠恕之名立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1208879_comment'></div>为人父而忠恕，则己与一家去道不远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1208879_comment'></div>为人君而忠恕，则己与天下国家去道不远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1208879_comment'></div>忠恕以人治，人犹己，肫肫其中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_107_1208879'>●「君子之道四，丘未能一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1208879_comment'></div>所求乎子以事父，未能也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1208879_comment'></div>所求乎臣以事君，未能也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1208879_comment'></div>所求乎弟以事兄，未能也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1208879_comment'></div>所求乎朋友先施之，未能也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1208879_comment'></div>中也诚也，教之所以为教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_113_1208879'>●「庸德之行，庸言之谨，有所不足，不敢不勉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1208879_comment'></div>有馀，不敢尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1208879_comment'></div>言顾行，行顾言，君子胡不慥慥尔」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1208879_comment'></div>中也诚也，道之所以为道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_117_1208879'>○●「君子素其位而行，不愿乎其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1208879_comment'></div>素富贵行乎富贵，素贫贱行乎贫贱，素夷狄行乎夷狄，素患难行乎患难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1208879_comment'></div>君子无入而不自得焉」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1208879_comment'></div>中也，诚明之徵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_121_1208879'>●「在上位不陵下，在下位不援上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1208879_comment'></div>正己而不求于人，则无怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1208879_comment'></div>上不怨天，下不尤人，故君子居易以俟命，小人行险以徼幸」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1208879_comment'></div>中也诚明之自治也，于是察乎上下，达于天地，无不安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1208879_comment'></div>曾子曰：「己虽不能，亦不以援人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1208879_comment'></div>盖援之为援者如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1208879_comment'></div>曾子又曰：「孝子之事亲也，居易以俟命，不与险行以徼幸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_128_1208879'>○●「子曰：射有似乎君子，失诸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/336/Comments/0")'>正鹄</span>，反求诸其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1208879_comment'></div>君子之道，譬如行远必自迩，譬如登高必自卑」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1208879_comment'></div>中也诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_131_1208879'>●「《诗》曰：妻子好合，如鼓瑟琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1208879_comment'></div>兄弟既翕，和乐且耽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1208879_comment'></div>宜尔室家，乐尔妻孥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1208879_comment'></div>子曰：父母其顺矣乎」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1208879_comment'></div>中为天下之大本，于是乎在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1208879_comment'></div>夫既得于父母，则室家宜之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_137_1208879'>○○●「子曰：鬼神之为德，其盛矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1208879_comment'></div>视之而弗见，听之而弗闻，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/360/Comments/0")'>体物</span>而不可遗，使天下之人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/362/Comments/0")'>齐明</span>盛服，以承祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1208879_comment'></div>洋洋乎如在其上，如在其左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1208879_comment'></div>诗曰：神之格思，不可度思，矧可射思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1208879_comment'></div>夫微之显，诚之不可掩如此夫」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1208879_comment'></div>中也，明诚无不达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_143_1208879'>○○●「子曰：舜其大孝也与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1208879_comment'></div>德为圣人，尊为天子，富有四海之内，宗庙飨之，子孙保之，故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_144_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/381/Comments/0")'>大德</span>必得其位，必得其禄，必得其名，必得其寿」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1208879_comment'></div>无闻焉尔也，疑简编缪于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_146_1208879'>●「故天之生物，必因其材而笃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1208879_comment'></div>故栽者培之，倾者覆之」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1208879_comment'></div>天之用中，因物而诚至焉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_149_1208879'>●「《诗》曰：嘉乐君子，宪宪令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1208879_comment'></div>宜民宜人，受禄于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1208879_comment'></div>保佑命之，自天申之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1208879_comment'></div>故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_152_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/400/Comments/1")'>大德</span>者必受命」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1208879_comment'></div>疑当次「必得其寿」之下，简编之缪也，无闻焉尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_154_1208879'>○○●「子曰：无忧者，其唯文王乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1208879_comment'></div>以王季为父，以武王为子，父作之，子述之」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1208879_comment'></div>无闻焉尔也，疑简编缪于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_157_1208879'>●「武王缵大王、王季、文王之绪，壹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_157_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/414/Comments/0")'>戎衣</span>而有天下，身不失天下之显名，尊为天子，富有四海之内，宗庙飨之，子孙保之」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1208879_comment'></div>无闻焉尔也，疑简编缪于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_159_1208879'>●「武王末受命，周公成文武之德，追王大王、王季，上祀先公以天子之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1208879_comment'></div>斯礼也，达乎诸侯大夫及士庶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1208879_comment'></div>父为大夫，子为士，葬以大夫，祭以士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1208879_comment'></div>父为士，子为大夫，葬以士，祭以大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1208879_comment'></div>期之丧，达乎大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1208879_comment'></div>三年之丧，达乎天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1208879_comment'></div>父母之丧，无贵贱一也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1208879_comment'></div>周公之所为周公者，中庸也，诚明两尽而道教行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_167_1208879'>○○●「子曰：武王、周公其达孝矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1208879_comment'></div>夫孝者善继人之志，善述人之事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1208879_comment'></div>春秋修其祖庙，陈其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_169_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/450/Comments/0")'>宗器</span>，设其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_169_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/451/Comments/0")'>裳衣</span>，荐其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_169_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/452/Comments/0")'>时食</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1208879_comment'></div>宗庙之礼，所以序昭穆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1208879_comment'></div>序爵所以辨贵贱也，序事所以辨贤也，旅酬下为上，所以逮贱也，燕毛所以序齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1208879_comment'></div>践其位，行其礼，奏其乐，敬其所尊，爱其所亲，事死如事生，事亡如事存，孝之至也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1208879_comment'></div>武王、周公之所以为武王、周公者，中庸也，诚明两尽而道教行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_174_1208879'>●「郊社之礼所以事上帝也，宗庙之礼所以祀乎其先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1208879_comment'></div>明乎郊社之礼，禘尝之义，治国其如示诸掌乎」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1208879_comment'></div>无闻焉尔也，疑简编脱缪于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1208879_comment'></div>尝有见于《仲尼燕居》也，文字又有误者，社无与于上帝也，陆淳尝辨此详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_178_1208879'>○○●「哀公问政，子曰：文武之政，布在方策，其人存则其政举，其人亡则其政息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1208879_comment'></div>人道敏政，地道敏树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1208879_comment'></div>夫政也者，蒲卢也，故为政在人，取人以身，修身以道，修道以仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1208879_comment'></div>仁者人也，亲亲为大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1208879_comment'></div>义者宜也，尊贤为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1208879_comment'></div>亲亲之杀，尊贤之等，礼所生也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1208879_comment'></div>中庸之政也，人道之勉乎，政犹地道之勉乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1208879_comment'></div>树艺稼穑也，中庸之政，感人心而迹自化，蒲卢之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1208879_comment'></div>仁义者，诚明之异名也，仁义合而礼生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1208879_comment'></div>礼也者，广骛驰骋于仁义之中者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_188_1208879'>●「在下位不获乎上，民不可得而治矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1208879_comment'></div>郑氏云：脱误重在此也，胡先生亦云然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_190_1208879'>●「故君子不可以不修身，思修身不可以不事亲，思事亲不可以不知人，思知人不可以不知天」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1208879_comment'></div>诚明始于身，本于亲，著于人，极于天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_192_1208879'>「天下之达道五，所以行之者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1208879_comment'></div>曰君臣也，父子也，夫妇也，昆弟也，朋友之交也，五者天下之达道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1208879_comment'></div>知、仁、勇三者，天下之达德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1208879_comment'></div>所以行之者一也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1208879_comment'></div>一于中也，达道之五行于达德之三，达德之三行于中之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1208879_comment'></div>达道者，修道之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_198_1208879'>○●「或生而知之，或学而知之，或困而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1208879_comment'></div>及其知之一也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1208879_comment'></div>一于中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_201_1208879'>●「或安而行之，或利而行之，或勉强而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1208879_comment'></div>及其成功一也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1208879_comment'></div>一于中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_204_1208879'>○○●「子曰：好学近乎知，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_204_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/556/Comments/0")'>力行</span>近乎仁，知耻近乎勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1208879_comment'></div>知斯三者，则知所以修身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1208879_comment'></div>知所以修身，则知所以治人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1208879_comment'></div>知所以治人，则知所以治天下国家矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1208879_comment'></div>达德之渐也，诚之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_209_1208879'>○●「凡为天下国家有九经：曰修身也，尊贤也，亲亲也，敬大臣也，体群臣也，子庶民也，来百工也，柔远人也，怀诸侯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1208879_comment'></div>修身则道立，尊贤则不惑，亲亲则诸父昆弟不怨，敬大臣则不眩，体群臣则士之报礼重，子庶民则百姓劝，来百工则财用足，柔远人则四方归之，怀诸侯则天下畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_211_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/585/Comments/0")'>齐明</span>盛服，非礼不动，所以修身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1208879_comment'></div>去谗远色，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_212_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/589/Comments/0")'>贱货</span>而贵德，所以劝贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1208879_comment'></div>尊其位，重其禄，同其好恶，所以劝亲亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1208879_comment'></div>官盛任使，所以劝大臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1208879_comment'></div>忠信重禄，所以劝士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1208879_comment'></div>时使薄歛，所以劝百姓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1208879_comment'></div>日省月试，既禀称事，所以劝百工也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_218_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/604/Comments/0")'>送往迎来</span>，嘉善而矜不能，所以柔远人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1208879_comment'></div>继绝世，举废国，治乱持危，朝聘以时，厚往而薄来，所以怀诸侯也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1208879_comment'></div>中庸之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1208879_comment'></div>问者曰：「如之何尊贤则不惑，敬大臣则不眩」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1208879_comment'></div>曰：谗色货能惑，我而不惑，则尊贤之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1208879_comment'></div>有百官之富任使，各尽其材，大臣凛然在上，天下名实不眩，则敬大臣之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1208879_comment'></div>不眩犹不惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_225_1208879'>○●「凡为天下国家有九经，所以行之者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1208879_comment'></div>凡事豫则立，不豫则废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1208879_comment'></div>言前定则不跲，事前定则不困，行前定则不疚，道前定则不穷」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1208879_comment'></div>诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1208879_comment'></div>诚则事前而豫，不诚则事至而无所图也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_230_1208879'>●○○「在下位不获乎上，民不可得而治矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1208879_comment'></div>获乎上有道，不信乎朋友，不获乎上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1208879_comment'></div>信乎朋友有道，不顺乎亲，不信乎朋友矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1208879_comment'></div>顺乎亲有道，反诸身不诚，不顺乎亲矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1208879_comment'></div>诚身有道，不明乎善，不诚乎身矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1208879_comment'></div>道必资乎诚，诚必资乎明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_236_1208879'>●「诚者天之道也，诚之者人之道也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1208879_comment'></div>兼天人之道而中庸著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1208879_comment'></div>舜诚矣，好问而好察迩言，隐恶而扬善，则诚之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1208879_comment'></div>颜回诚矣，得一善则拳拳服膺而弗失之者，诚之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_240_1208879'>●「诚者不勉而中，不思而得，从容中道，圣人也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1208879_comment'></div>天之道也，中道而未从容，则贤人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_242_1208879'>●「诚之者，择善而固执之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_243_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/673/Comments/0")'>博学</span>之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_243_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/674/Comments/0")'>审问</span>之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_243_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/675/Comments/0")'>慎思</span>之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_243_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/676/Comments/0")'>明辨</span>之，笃行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1208879_comment'></div>有弗学，学之弗能，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1208879_comment'></div>有弗问，问之弗知，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1208879_comment'></div>有弗思，思之弗得，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1208879_comment'></div>有弗辨，辨之弗明，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1208879_comment'></div>有弗行，行之弗笃，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1208879_comment'></div>人一能之，己百之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1208879_comment'></div>人十能之，己千之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1208879_comment'></div>果能此道矣，虽愚必明，虽柔必强」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1208879_comment'></div>人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_253_1208879'>○○●「自诚明谓之性，自明诚谓之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1208879_comment'></div>诚则明矣，明则诚矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1208879_comment'></div>诚明各有所致而相为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1208879_comment'></div>四时诚矣，较然著见，则自诚而明之性也，犹天命之性也，日月明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1208879_comment'></div>其出入有信，则明而诚之教也，犹脩道之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1208879_comment'></div>未有诚而不明者也，未有明而不诚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1208879_comment'></div>彼偏焉者，非诚明之正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1208879_comment'></div>武王、周公以孝称，则举其自诚明者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1208879_comment'></div>舜以知称，则举其自明诚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1208879_comment'></div>非有圣贤之差也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_263_1208879'>○●「唯天下至诚为能尽其性，能尽其性则能尽人之性，能尽人之性则能尽物之性，能尽物之性则可以赞天地之化育，可以赞天地之化育则可以与天地参矣」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1208879_comment'></div>率性以诚也，人物之性与天地之化育皆吾性之诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1208879_comment'></div>天地之性不可见，而见之于化育也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1208879_comment'></div>然此非次第而言之也，犹曰能尽其性则能尽人之性，则能尽物之性，则能赞天地之化育，而与天地参也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1208879_comment'></div>其所言之若是者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1208879_comment'></div>视其相因者殷勤之也，非心知其意者，莫之能喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1208879_comment'></div>物性之粗，非后于人之性而得之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_270_1208879'>○●「其次致曲，曲能有诚，诚则形，形则著，著则明，明则动，动则变，变则化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1208879_comment'></div>唯天下至诚为能化」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1208879_comment'></div>无闻焉尔也，胡先生亦所不讲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1208879_comment'></div>是自诚而明者谓之次焉，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1208879_comment'></div>郑氏乃谓自明诚者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_275_1208879'>●「至诚之道可以前知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1208879_comment'></div>国家将兴，必有祯祥，国家将亡，必有妖孽，见乎蓍龟，动乎四体，祸福将至，善必先知之，不善必先知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1208879_comment'></div>故至诚如神」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1208879_comment'></div>无闻焉尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1208879_comment'></div>胡先生、温公、姚子张皆疑之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1208879_comment'></div>明道先生曰：「诚者神也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1208879_comment'></div>盖从明道先生之说，则何必如之云也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_282_1208879'>○●「诚者自成也，而道自道也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1208879_comment'></div>诚与道一体而二名也，其所以率性则一也，皆无待于外者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_284_1208879'>●「诚者物之终始，不诚无物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1208879_comment'></div>是故君子诚之为贵」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1208879_comment'></div>温公曰：凡物自始至终，诚实有之，乃能为物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1208879_comment'></div>若其不诚，则皆无之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_288_1208879'>●「诚者非自成己而已也，所以成物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1208879_comment'></div>成己仁也，成物知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1208879_comment'></div>性之德也，合外内之道也，故时措之宜也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1208879_comment'></div>物者己之物也，己与物非有二也，皆其诚之物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1208879_comment'></div>成己斯成物也，唯所措而宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1208879_comment'></div>圣人之道，所以异乎杨墨者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1208879_comment'></div>成己知也，乃谓之曰仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1208879_comment'></div>成物仁也，乃谓之曰知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_296_1208879'>○●「故至诚无息，不息则久，久则徵，徵则悠远，悠远则博厚，博厚则高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1208879_comment'></div>博厚所以载物也，高明所以覆物也，悠久所以成物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1208879_comment'></div>博厚配地，高明配天，悠久无疆，如此者不见而章，不动而变，无为而成天地之道，可一言而尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1208879_comment'></div>其为物不贰，则其生物不测」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1208879_comment'></div>诚明之极，配天地而一之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1208879_comment'></div>诚斯一也，一斯诚也，此盖当云徵则博厚，博厚则高明，高明则悠远，考下文而不诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1208879_comment'></div>夫言天地之体，则高明博厚而足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1208879_comment'></div>人之体乎天地之高明博厚，则必待悠久以为之中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1208879_comment'></div>盖非悠久之中，则其高明将隳，博厚将蹶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1208879_comment'></div>博厚高明，譬诸形体也，悠久譬诸精神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1208879_comment'></div>曾子曰：「君子尊其所闻则高明矣，行其所闻则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_306_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/844/Comments/0")'>广大</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1208879_comment'></div>高明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_307_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/845/Comments/0")'>广大</span>不在于他，在加之至而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_307_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/846/Comments/1")'>已矣</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1208879_comment'></div>夫曾子所谓至者，子思所谓悠久是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1208879_comment'></div>曰悠远，曰悠久，其实同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1208879_comment'></div>夫不见不动无为者中也，既章既变既成则亦中也，此不二之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_311_1208879'>●「天地之道博也，厚也，高也，明也，悠也，久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_312_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/861/Comments/0")'>今夫</span>天，斯昭昭之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1208879_comment'></div>及其无穷也，日月星辰系焉，万物覆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_314_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/866/Comments/0")'>今夫</span>地，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_314_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/867/Comments/0")'>一撮</span>土之多，及其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_314_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/868/Comments/0")'>广厚</span>，载<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_314_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/869/Comments/0")'>华岳</span>而不重，振河海而不泄，万物载焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_315_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/872/Comments/0")'>今夫</span>山，一<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_315_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/873/Comments/0")'>卷石</span>之多，及其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_315_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/874/Comments/0")'>广大</span>，草木生之，禽兽居之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_315_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/877/Comments/0")'>宝藏</span>兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1208879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_316_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/878/Comments/0")'>今夫</span>水，一勺之多，及其不测，鼋鼍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_316_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/881/Comments/0")'>蛟龙</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_316_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/881/Comments/1")'>鱼鳖</span>生焉，货财殖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1208879_comment'></div>《诗》云：『维天之命，于穆不已』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1208879_comment'></div>盖曰天之所以为天也，于乎不显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1208879_comment'></div>文王之德之纯，盖曰文王之所以为文也，纯亦不已」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1208879_comment'></div>天地圣人之悠久一也，博厚高明之所资以为中者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_321_1208879'>○○●「大哉圣人之道，洋洋乎，发育万物，峻极于天，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_321_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/897/Comments/0")'>优优</span>大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1208879_comment'></div>礼仪三百，威仪三千，待其人而后行，故曰苟不至德，至道不凝焉」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1208879_comment'></div>圣人之高明博厚悠久，一之于中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1208879_comment'></div>中者至德是也，发育万物，峻极于天，高明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1208879_comment'></div>礼仪三百，威仪三千，博厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1208879_comment'></div>待其人而后行，悠久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1208879_comment'></div>至道高明博厚也，至德悠久也，至道至德犹达道达德也，明道先生谓此一以贯之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_328_1208879'>●「故君子尊德性而道问学，致<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_328_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/919/Comments/0")'>广大</span>而尽精微，极高明而道中庸，温故而知新，敦厚以崇礼」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1208879_comment'></div>率性修道于是乎极也，思尊德性而必道问学，问学斯德性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1208879_comment'></div>思致<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_330_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/926/Comments/0")'>广大</span>而必尽精微，精微斯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_330_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/927/Comments/0")'>广大</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1208879_comment'></div>思极高明而必道中庸，中庸斯高明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1208879_comment'></div>思温故而必知新，知新斯温故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1208879_comment'></div>思敦厚而必崇礼，崇礼斯敦厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1208879_comment'></div>德性犹悠久也，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_334_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/935/Comments/0")'>广大</span>犹博厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1208879_comment'></div>胡先生、二程先生及横渠先生说皆同，近世瞽学谓既极高明而反道中庸，末乎中庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1208879_comment'></div>分而为二事，莫知诚之一致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_337_1208879'>○●「是故居上不骄，为下不倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1208879_comment'></div>国有道，其言足以兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1208879_comment'></div>国无道，其默足以容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1208879_comment'></div>《诗》曰『既明且哲，以保其身』，其斯之谓与」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1208879_comment'></div>中也，明之所安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_342_1208879'>○●「子曰：愚而好自用，贱而好自专，生乎今之世，反古之道，如此者，灾及其身者也」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1208879_comment'></div>不明之患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1208879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_344_1208879'>○●「非天子不议礼，不制度，不考文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1208879_comment'></div>今天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_345_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/963/Comments/0")'>车同轨</span>，书同文，行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_345_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/965/Comments/0")'>同伦</span>，虽有其位，苟无其德，不敢作礼乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1208879_comment'></div>虽有其德，苟无其位，亦不敢作礼乐焉」者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1208879_comment'></div>思教之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1208879_comment'></div>今天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_348_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/973/Comments/0")'>车同轨</span>，贵贱无等也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1208879_comment'></div>书同文，是非杂出也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1208879_comment'></div>行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_350_1208879", 1208879, "Clauses/977/Comments/0")'>同伦</span>，君子小人并列也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1208879_comment'></div>礼乐之中庸，莫之有作也，胡先生说云尔也。<div class='inline'
