-----title
成县（同谷）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a73d4722c5e24cff9c3e7e2905770968_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a73d4722c5e24cff9c3e7e2905770968");'><span id='a73d4722c5e24cff9c3e7e2905770968_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1124')">1121-1124年</a>，63-66岁</div><div id='a73d4722c5e24cff9c3e7e2905770968' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　初春，赴任成州知州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　朝请大夫，知成州军事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　清明游成县南狮子洞并题名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　四月作文。作品：《康节先生谥议后记》<div id='poem_1208806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>康节先生谥议后记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208806")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208806'>说之大观四年庚寅冬赴明州船场，候潮浙江上，遇欧阳三丈叔弼，相与遨游谈话旬日，甚乐，因及三丈所作《康节先生谥议》，三丈曰：「异哉，吾之斯文也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208806_comment'></div>何吾以道爱之深邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208806_comment'></div>曰：「丈人斯文可谓合矣，何异之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208806_comment'></div>曰：「姑听之，棐从母王宣徽夫人得疾洛阳，先妣夫人亟以棐入洛，时先公参大政，临行告戒曰：『洛中有邵尧夫，吾独不识，汝为吾见之』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208806_comment'></div>棐既至洛，自幸得见先生，何期赐之从容，则起问其所以宜教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208806_comment'></div>先生笑曰：『有家法，有家法』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208806_comment'></div>既乃作而言曰：『岂无以为足下言者』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208806_comment'></div>先生乃徐道其立身本末，苦辛备细，毕平生于一席端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208806_comment'></div>出门揖送，犹曰：『足下其无忘鄙野之人于异日』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208806_comment'></div>棐伏念行李间，先生岂不少我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208806_comment'></div>未尝辱教一言，虽欲不忘，亦何事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208806_comment'></div>归白大人，则喜曰：『幸矣，邵尧夫有以处吾儿也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208806_comment'></div>其后二十年，棐偶入太常为博士，次当作先生谥议，乃恍然周省先生当时之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208806_comment'></div>落笔若先生之自序云尔，无待其家所上文字也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208806_comment'></div>叔弼丈为人廉于名誉，俛俛常有退让之色，其为说之道此时，意气甚武，宜其文之健且高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208806_comment'></div>说之谢曰：「昔郭景纯先知行刑者，吾康节先生知谥议博士，迹则类矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208806_comment'></div>然郭以术，先生则孰知其所以然邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208806_comment'></div>叔弼丈曰：「世称先生数学如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208806_comment'></div>说之复言曰：「先生传先天之数，虽扬雄、张衡、关子明所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208806_comment'></div>然亦吾先生《易》中一事也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208806_comment'></div>叔弼丈叹曰：「先生之《易》毕，能悉备如是，盍为我道之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208806_comment'></div>说之辞不敏，且不幸不及先生之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208806_comment'></div>而为《京氏易》十馀年后，遇先生门人洛阳杨宝贤，略能发先生《易》之梗概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208806_comment'></div>久之乃有所入，则知先生起卦以四，是谓夏时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208806_comment'></div>以六，是谓《坤》、《乾》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208806_comment'></div>以八，是谓《周易》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208806_comment'></div>先生使夏商之《易》不亡，而《周易》、《乾》、《夬》之变始终不穷，犹丈人之作谥议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208806_comment'></div>叔弼丈复谢曰：「吾之文于是乎陋矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208806_comment'></div>嗟夫，岁复一星矣，三丈下世已累年，追惟故人，存者有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208806_comment'></div>先生之子伯温又远守南充，以书来趣说之记其事，不得而辞云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208806_comment'></div>宣和四年四月丙申，成州清心堂嵩山晁说之记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1208806'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1208806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　十一月十一日作文。作品：《文林启秀序》<div id='poem_1208788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文林启秀序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208788")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208788'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208788'>说之曾大父文庄公，少因文元公而行辈高，与一时文士周旋，安知有刑名学，而纠察刑狱、判审刑院、知开封府，振疑奋滞，如狱具中不得死者十人，而法不胜情，伏重罪者一二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208788_comment'></div>其为学士也，一夕行王章惠、陈文思、张邓公、章郇公、盛文肃公五将相制，不废麻卷三鼓之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208788_comment'></div>而先对灾异者久之，以手诏使陕西，折夏英公、韩魏公、范文正公、尹师鲁、田宣简公之谋，遂参知政事，上专以西事委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208788_comment'></div>公尽瘁匪躬，知无不言，罢夏英公、陈恭公经略招讨使，分秦凤、泾原、环庆、鄜延为四路，讫今不可改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208788_comment'></div>公陈边策于昊贼未叛之前，而卒如公策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208788_comment'></div>其招纳昊贼之时，公薨矣，悲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208788_comment'></div>公以家族保范文正公擅遗昊贼书无他，明刘平、石元孙战殁非降贼，获褒赠，辩宋莒公、郑文肃、叶道卿、龙图阁直学士吴安道非朋党，不以罪贬，则公之姿度闳远，早擅岩廊之望焉者，于是乎称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208788_comment'></div>然公于学则微悉密致，与癯儒等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208788_comment'></div>尝以《文选》、《续文选》、《艺文类聚》、《初学记》、《文苑英华》、南北朝洎隋唐人之文集，美字粹语，分百七十有四门，十卷，名之曰《文林启秀》，玩之发人藻思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208788_comment'></div>目无遗物，动涉芳尘，如游玉田芝房，其名曰「启秀」宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208788_comment'></div>昔稽叔夜喜音韵学，谢康乐疲于译梵字，颜鲁公老于韵海，皆天下雄伟超杰之资而谨小德，绳墨不屑也，吾曾大父何疑焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208788_comment'></div>嗟乎，今之文务为高论，以扬子云雕虫篆刻藉口，而心不知卫武公切瑳琢磨者何事，其体物曲成，则又何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208788_comment'></div>说之何知，敢序之，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208788_comment'></div>宣和四年十一月十一日乙丑，朝请大夫、知成州晁说之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1208788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在成州，赐紫金鱼袋，乞宫观，不与。成州秋旱，减免民税，激怒转运使，上书申辩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在成州。作品：《题戒杀生文后》《题长编疑事》《荐薄君刊曹书》《送屈用诚序》《与宋运使书》《岁暮绝句四首》<div id='poem_1208813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题戒杀生文后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208813")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208813'>说之窃闻国史《钱内翰传》称著《杀生戒》后，吾祖文元赞之，推广其意，史官是以知仁泽之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208813_comment'></div>然史官不言钱公策试贤良方正时，实吾祖文元公为其主司，公忘去辈行以奖善，其用意尤深切矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208813_comment'></div>或曰：史官之书曰「文元公后见而赞之」，益广其意，非欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208813_comment'></div>莫得而详已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208813_comment'></div>慈云当是时与三公甚厚，宜其德名今犹凛然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208813_comment'></div>宣和五年癸卯四月戊申，晁说之再刻板，谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1208813_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题长编疑事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年5月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208805")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208805'>《长编》者，温公《资治通鉴》藁草之私号也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208805_comment'></div>温公自洛中以所修藁草寄其属官南康军监酒刘道原，而自名之欤，抑道原之名欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208805_comment'></div>道原日诵万言，而勤废饮食寝处，遂忘其身之流落而家寒饿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208805_comment'></div>其忠愤耿介，当熙宁初，不为大丞相毫发少贬者，虽自其天姿，亦博学精思之助哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208805_comment'></div>观斯《疑事》，则其闳远沈粹之躅，亦略可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208805_comment'></div>《通鉴》之为书，有贤杰辅相攻坚析微如此，安得不善邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208805_comment'></div>昔其初不自珍，而公卧病二年之久，家人单弱忧瘁之中幸而存者，姑五十有五种也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208805_comment'></div>公之子羲仲壮舆，政和戊戌为唐州曹官，录以寄说之东里草堂，初拜嘉而不甚器之，以壮舆作《资治通鉴考异》，待其异日之成书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208805_comment'></div>今壮舆死已累年，斯事已矣，谁能措手？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208805_comment'></div>不觉涕泪无从，渍于残缺仅存之书，嗟嗟良友，奕世厚善之意，实存于其中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208805_comment'></div>重惟壮舆临终属我铭其墓，久难之未就，乃先以摅予之哀云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208805_comment'></div>宣和五年癸卯五月二十六日戊寅，嵩山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1208805_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208776' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208776' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208776?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送屈用诚序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年12月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208776")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208776_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208776'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208776'>屈鼎画山水，当时与范宽齐名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208776_comment'></div>其后范之名日盛，而屈或不得与，良可叹也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208776_comment'></div>范之笔突兀而易识，学者自谓易为范也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208776_comment'></div>屈则沈毅横恣，几绝来学之路，非笃志老于其事者，鲜不忽诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208776_comment'></div>如纪真、黄怀玉、商训辈皆学范而大得名者，未知有一人称屈之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208776_comment'></div>惟是其家子孙自致身于遗踪间而珍之，不肯少贬于众好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208776_comment'></div>孙用诚者得其法为多，老矣，衣食贫，所踬每为人作其老阿父画，遇十人而九不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208776_comment'></div>用诚曰：「奈何，要当疗饥寒于速售者，无如许家父近之为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208776_comment'></div>许道宁云：「尔劣为许家父画，视一人则十百人争赏之，恐不得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208776_comment'></div>用诚叹曰：「吾虽饱于许家父，暖于许家父，其如吾志之饥且寒何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208776_comment'></div>复恐地下无见吾老阿父之面目也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208776_comment'></div>以故栖栖岐山下，东未尝至咸阳，宁论京师贵人之媚哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208776_comment'></div>予前年道扶风，偶见用诚之屏障而多之，力致之于同谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208776_comment'></div>初为予作画犹是许家父也，予斥之曰：「老处士非蓊云屈郎之孙也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208776_comment'></div>乃瞿然亟作其老阿父八幅而告归，予勉之曰：「尔祖卒年九十有四岁，未死前数日犹画不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208776_comment'></div>尔年方将七十岁，未宜自怠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208776_comment'></div>古今学士大夫或遇不遇于一时，而遗恨于无穷者，正如尔祖与范之盛衰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208776_comment'></div>画知有吴而不知有张，书知有王而不知有钟，儒生持子书而不读《孝经》，可胜道哉，可胜道哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208776_comment'></div>岁暮冰雪，用诚复徒步还岐山下，予亟序以送之，可为我示令君吕二十一郎，是一门四相家，必有以感于予之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208776_comment'></div>宣和癸卯十二月三日，嵩山晁说之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1208776_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与宋运使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年12月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208750")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208750'>说之敢言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208750_comment'></div>昨日荐蒲贽人回，独蒙教答，何胜感仄！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208750_comment'></div>此外复有职事，谨用汉制敢言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208750_comment'></div>本州今年秋旱，同谷县人户所诉二万五千馀灾，其所检校放者一万三千馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208750_comment'></div>栗亭县诉一万三千馀灾，而检放者八千五百馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208750_comment'></div>说之无状，唯知夙夜愧恨，深负斯民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208750_comment'></div>负斯民于下可也，其如上无以称圣君仁惠远降御香、闵雨祈祷、轸恤元元之意何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208750_comment'></div>属者运句冯从事入境，道路諠言，正为税事而来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208750_comment'></div>说之无状，窃彷徨自叹息曰：「死矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208750_comment'></div>放税不如百姓之所欲，将得罪于明使者，吾何面目在人间生活耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208750_comment'></div>且乱山丛溪之间，蕞然一郡，不识使台贵属来临者，累年其久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208750_comment'></div>今一旦老幼扶携，切切昂首，以听使属增放税数，以丑饥鹰刺史、饿虎县令，可以风威百城，岂不幸甚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208750_comment'></div>既而大不其然，乃是恶所放之过优，而欲令复之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208750_comment'></div>嗟乎，天壤之间，好恶不同，取舍顿异，一至此耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208750_comment'></div>是必非明府之意，而勾官失辞而然尔，顾岂不为明府累耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208750_comment'></div>前者疲瘵之民所以不至流徙，亦不甚阙食者，以所放之税粗能畔岸之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208750_comment'></div>苟若复之，或少镌削之，是网罗于前而捕扼于后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208750_comment'></div>方欲哺杯案而夺之手指也，其为守者平日粗与民有信，今则不胜其欺且罔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208750_comment'></div>设常有沮洳之泽，亦无以补斯炎炽之酷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208750_comment'></div>困之如彼，伐之如此，古人之所痛者，今宁不一动心也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208750_comment'></div>所谓结怨于一州，取笑于朝廷者，又于今日而见之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208750_comment'></div>窃复自念，平居乡闾，饿死不贰吾言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208750_comment'></div>今兹假守以褊小之地，遂使难为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208750_comment'></div>盖必欲蹙之，首鼠无他也，素不自重，不诚于身，则不获于上，而下亦莫我获也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208750_comment'></div>夫鸷鸟在上，重鼎在下，不程勇力，不悔其往，不豫其来，儒者之细事，患不自勉，且不自信尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208750_comment'></div>昔舒仲应为沛相，袁术以米十万斛为沛军粮，仲应以给饥民，术怒欲斩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208750_comment'></div>仲应曰：「知当必死，故为之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208750_comment'></div>宁可以一人之命，救百姓于涂炭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208750_comment'></div>术谢之曰：「仲应足下独欲享天下重名，不与吾共之耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208750_comment'></div>彼袁术者，人之豺狼者也，方与群雄血战之时，乃知出此，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208750_comment'></div>仲应之米十万斛，今兹杂色不当其十之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208750_comment'></div>况明府素不畏高明，则不虐茕独矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208750_comment'></div>说之窃恃明府而安之不贰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208750_comment'></div>目前似少鲁国男子，或为孱守而危者，不知明府者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208750_comment'></div>或曰，其如<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺）</span>何曰岂无策哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208750_comment'></div>说之老矣，乞宫观既不谐，行当乞放罢东归，如明府未赐斥绝，尚当于明府布露之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208750_comment'></div>区区所见，实系事体，可以实塞下而富国中，明府必将乐乎听之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208750_comment'></div>伏惟运使大卿财幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208750_comment'></div>十二月十八日，知成州晁说之敢言之。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1208750'></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1208750_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196769?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岁暮绝句四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_196769")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196769'>卫霍功名无素誉，韩彭富贵晚堪悲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196769'>梅花引角边情剧，况复人间岁暮时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196769'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196769_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196768' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196768' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196768?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196768_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196768'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196768'>下惠一时行已志，首阳万古振人伦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196768'>终南不得西山号，岁暮白头空断魂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196768'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196768_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196767' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196767' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196767?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196767_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196767'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196767'>沉沉欲雪岫云平，月尾年头此有情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196767'>童稚欢欣学秦语，不知家世本东京。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196767'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196767_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196766?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196766'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196766'>迟迟来日去何疾，六十五见此日除。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196766'>明发束修能有几，太平田舍读残书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196766'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　在成州时，与郭执中唱和甚多。作品：《再和圆机喜雪之作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《嵩山文集》卷八有与圆机唱和诗60余首，不俱列。）</span><div id='poem_197071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再和圆机喜雪之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197071")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197071'>十遇荒饥一遇丰，人间不见壁间龙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197071'>既悭雨泽空仓厄，仍广车舆小子封。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197071'>俗吏教条徒自愧，滮池云物幸相容。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197071'>怪来不与秦湫诅，应许多藏汉大农<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197071'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_197071_0'>⑴ 自注：秦名池曰湫，皆投以诅楚文，今此池独不与也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197071_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州（高邮）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5bc06e6cadfa4bc7affb9953dc5dadd7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5bc06e6cadfa4bc7affb9953dc5dadd7");'><span id='5bc06e6cadfa4bc7affb9953dc5dadd7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1127')">1126-1127年</a>，68-69岁</div><div id='5bc06e6cadfa4bc7affb9953dc5dadd7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　十二月，到达高邮。作品：《答钟离中远先辈书》<div id='poem_1208764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答钟离中远先辈书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208764")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208764_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208764'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208764'>说之启：老益迂拙，无以立朝，上辜睿奖，招谗被逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208764_comment'></div>方出国门俟命之际，遽闻胡骑渡河，苍黄觅舟东下，至睢阳，舟欲行而河绝流，始知古人欲济无航之叹，于我未甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208764_comment'></div>既而闻胡虏破拱州，将攻睢阳，遂舍舟，与凡百士族民伍杂然奔亡，朝雨暮云，饥不知寒，仅有竹舆，不如徒步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208764_comment'></div>既过之处，胡寇与溃兵踵迹相接，若来追逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208764_comment'></div>而彼方嗜杀略焚荡，使我得以小舟渡淮，至高邮，见其可居，而不顾其不可居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208764_comment'></div>匆匆来觅亲旧，少以生民自置尔，敢期足下惠然以长书宠临，究惟平昔蝉联之契，足下过误之闻，而得文彩焕耀，坐还太平士夫之风仪，岂不幸甚，非常日比也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208764_comment'></div>虽然，足下知德而未知人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208764_comment'></div>仆无状，不能自立于图治之朝，而少居构乱之乡，妻孥方且耻笑，足下乃处以前辈典刑，无乃为足下知德之累乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208764_comment'></div>仆今日危邦必入，乱邦必居，无知之小人也，尚何足与语？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208764_comment'></div>然或可因法语之言以谢盛意，病者未必不知药也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208764_comment'></div>夫所谓危邦不入者，岂不谓不苟得而求利也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208764_comment'></div>箕子之明夷是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208764_comment'></div>乱邦不居，则宁杀吾身以谏吾君，而不使吾邦祸乱以亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208764_comment'></div>比干之死是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208764_comment'></div>苟以谓避危而去乱，则吾君孰与居者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208764_comment'></div>又孰与守者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208764_comment'></div>吾父母之邦，无异羁旅之舍也，小雅怨刺之士，肯出此言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208764_comment'></div>足下以谓如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208764_comment'></div>足下旦夕间绝浙江，游会稽，访谢安石、王逸少之故栖，必有忠厚君子因足下而知吾言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208764_comment'></div>足下强学自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208764_comment'></div>十二月十一日，箕山晁说之上先辈钟离君足下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1208764_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1127')">1126-1127年</a>　在高邮。作品：《洪范小传》《题七贤图》《题江南后主词翰》《题蔡君谟吊石曼卿诗后》《跋忠懿王草圣》《题鲁直尝新柑帖》《题东坡试袁绍先笔借登真隐诀》《题鲁直章草颠草》《题东坡诗》《南门》《舟子语》《寄城中亲旧》《淮口作》《初到高邮》《穷途》《题破琴诗后》《题无水池新砚》《题黄龙山僧送善澄上人诗卷》《大辨》《跋李太白草书》《书与郭寿》《答张颐先辈书》《陈键字子感序》《寓高邮禅居寺》《春书》《高邮忽见叔易嵩山下所寄绝句……》《高邮书事》《三月五日，南京梢工来报……》<div id='poem_1208874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪范小传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208874")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208874'>「惟十有三祀，王访于箕子」：先《武成》以事天，后《洪范》以极天道，不称周年而称商祀，就箕子以访焉，则武成所谓乃反商政，政由旧者，于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208874_comment'></div>武王若曰：箕子者，吾商之旧三公也，吾欲有闻则访焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1208874'>「帝乃震怒，不畀」：不畀者，不与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208874_comment'></div>帝之不与鲧者，鲧失治道于天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208874_comment'></div>故声其恶曰：「彝伦攸斁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208874_comment'></div>迹其不畀之实曰：「鲧则殛死，禹乃嗣兴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208874_comment'></div>禹嗣鲧之职，而鲧之所不举者，一日兴起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208874_comment'></div>旧说废父与子者误也，其意私且狭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208874_comment'></div>「天乃锡禹」者，锡其所兴也，锡则畀之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208874_comment'></div>「《洪范》九畴，彝伦攸叙」者，天人德之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1208874'>「初一曰五行」：五行得其叙，是谓「彝伦攸叙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208874_comment'></div>土爰稼穑，水之润下，火之炎上，木之曲直，金之从革，皆具于土矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208874_comment'></div>土何事之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208874_comment'></div>其于稼穑则从人之欲而无不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208874_comment'></div>爰，曰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1208874'>「润下作咸，炎上作苦，曲直作酸，从革作辛，稼穑作甘」：润下作咸，水，咸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208874_comment'></div>炎上作苦，火，苦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208874_comment'></div>曲直作酸，木，酸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208874_comment'></div>从革作辛，金，辛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208874_comment'></div>稼穑作甘，土，甘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1208874'>「二、五事」：「一曰貌」，木也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208874_comment'></div>「二曰言」，金也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208874_comment'></div>「三曰视」，火也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208874_comment'></div>「四曰听」，水也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208874_comment'></div>「五曰思」，土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1208874'>「三、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1208874", 1208874, "Clauses/79/Comments/3")'>八政</span>」：「一曰食，二曰货，三曰祀」，五行之具用也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208874_comment'></div>「四曰司空」，水也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208874_comment'></div>「五曰司徒」，土也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208874_comment'></div>「六曰司寇」，金也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208874_comment'></div>「七曰宾」，木也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208874_comment'></div>「八曰师」，火也<span class='inlineComment2'>（下缺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1208874'><span class='inlineComment2'>（上缺。）</span>保之极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208874_comment'></div>「无偏无陂，遵王之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208874_comment'></div>无有作好，遵王之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208874_comment'></div>无有作恶，遵王之路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208874_comment'></div>无偏无党，王道荡荡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208874_comment'></div>无党无偏，王道平平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208874_comment'></div>无反无侧，王道正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208874_comment'></div>会其有极，归其有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208874_comment'></div>曰皇极之敷言，是彝是训，于帝其训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208874_comment'></div>凡厥庶民，极之敷言，是训是行，以近天子之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208874_comment'></div>曰天子作民父母，以为天下王」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208874_comment'></div>言人君人臣所以作极之术如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208874_comment'></div>人君之极，极于上帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208874_comment'></div>庶民之极，极于吾君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208874_comment'></div>「钦时五福，用敷锡厥庶民」，「凡厥正人，既富方谷，汝弗能使有好于而家，时人斯其辜，于其无好德，汝虽锡之福，其作汝用咎」，当次于「五福」之畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1208874'>「六、三德」：「一曰正直」，土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208874_comment'></div>「二曰刚克」，火也，金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208874_comment'></div>「三曰柔克」，水也，木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208874_comment'></div>「平康正直」，同土用土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208874_comment'></div>「疆弗友刚克」，因水木用火金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208874_comment'></div>「燮友柔克」，因火金用水木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208874_comment'></div>「沉潜刚克」，因水用火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208874_comment'></div>「高明柔克」，因火用水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208874_comment'></div>「惟辟作福，惟辟作威，惟辟玉食，臣无有作福作威玉食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208874_comment'></div>臣之有作福作威玉食，其害于而家，凶于而国，人用侧颇僻，民用僭忒」，当次于「五福」之畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1208874'>「七、稽疑」：「曰雨」，木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208874_comment'></div>「曰霁」，火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208874_comment'></div>「曰蒙」，金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208874_comment'></div>「曰驿」，水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208874_comment'></div>「曰克」，土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208874_comment'></div>「曰贞，曰悔」，五行具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208874_comment'></div>蒙，金文作雺，天气下地不应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208874_comment'></div>驿，今文作圛，升云半有半无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208874_comment'></div>克，于龟象五行交相，尧与土之状相类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1208874'>「八、庶徵」：「曰雨」，木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208874_comment'></div>「曰旸」，金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208874_comment'></div>「曰燠」，火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208874_comment'></div>「曰寒」，水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208874_comment'></div>「曰风」，土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208874_comment'></div>「曰肃，时雨若」，木以类从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208874_comment'></div>「曰哲，时燠若」，火以类从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208874_comment'></div>「曰谋，时寒若」，水以类从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208874_comment'></div>「曰圣，时风若」，土以类从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208874_comment'></div>咎徵「曰狂，恒雨若」，木自咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208874_comment'></div>「曰僭，恒旸若」，金自咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208874_comment'></div>「曰豫，恒燠若」，火自咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208874_comment'></div>「曰急，恒寒若」，水自咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1208874_comment'></div>「曰蒙，恒风若」，土自咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1208874_comment'></div>「曰王省惟岁，卿士惟月，师尹惟日，岁月日时无易，百谷用成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1208874_comment'></div>乂用明，俊民用章，家用平康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1208874_comment'></div>日月岁时既易，百谷用不成，乂用昏不明，俊民用徵，家用不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1208874_comment'></div>庶民惟星，星有好风，星有好雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1208874_comment'></div>日月之行，则有冬有夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1208874_comment'></div>月之从星，则以风雨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1208874_comment'></div>当次「五纪」之畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_1208874'>「九、五福」：「一曰寿」，土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1208874_comment'></div>「二曰富」，水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1208874_comment'></div>「三曰康宁」，火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1208874_comment'></div>「四曰攸好德」，木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1208874_comment'></div>「五曰考终命」，金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1208874_comment'></div>惟五福实亦备用，如寿富而康宁，康宁而寿富，攸好德而考终命，考终命而寿富之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1208874_comment'></div>「六极」：「一曰凶短折」，土也，金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1208874_comment'></div>「二曰疾」，火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1208874_comment'></div>「三曰忧」，火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1208874_comment'></div>「四曰贫」，水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1208874_comment'></div>「五曰恶」，木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1208874_comment'></div>「六曰弱」木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_1208874'>说之二十年前为《洪范》之学，本诸伏生、刘向、一行，而古今之说不敢遗也，为传数千言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1208874_comment'></div>靖康丙午冬遇金贼于睢阳，五世图书悉以灰烬，宁知有吾之《洪范传》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1208874_comment'></div>今年戊申冬飘流金陵，遇东里好学后生，尝标记予传之五行于本书，予欣然见之，如睹再生之物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1208874_comment'></div>方抱病危弱，于冬至前一日因作此小传，自安其私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1208874_comment'></div>而念学者之益，良亦未易议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1208874_comment'></div>二十二日壬寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1208874_comment'></div>至其次序，则多本诸泰山姜至之先生，论五行则张廷评景发之云<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_104_1208874'></div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1208874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1208874'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_104_1208874_0'>⑴ 《嵩山文集》卷一一。又见《经义考》卷九六，《宋元学案补遗》卷二二。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1208874_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1208816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题七贤图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208816")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208816'>评书曰非钟则王，岂知书者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208816_comment'></div>画之张、吴可同日语耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208816_comment'></div>黄七兄老矣，不得不昏缪如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208816_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1208816'>或谓此本唐人所摹，借以为高欤，实仰之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208816_comment'></div>观其点睛不着意，而手柔衣宽，非唐人脱笔之妙，莫之及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208816_comment'></div>靖康元年十一月二十日阻冻睢阳舟中题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1208816_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题江南后主词翰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208824")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208824'>黄鲁直谓李后主书出于裴休，予初大骇之，惟见休石刻字故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208824_comment'></div>晚乃见休行书墨迹一帖，良以愧叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208824_comment'></div>靖康元年丙午十二月二十六日，箕山晁说之避地于高邮题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208824_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题蔡君谟吊石曼卿诗后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年12月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208823")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208823'>蔡公于是乎句法曼卿，而字尽曼卿，真足以吊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208823_comment'></div>靖康元年十一月二十三日，嵩山晁说之题睢阳舟中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1208823_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋忠懿王草圣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208817")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208817'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208817'>荆南王修撰作《五朝春秋》，托始于吴越，犹之鲁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208817_comment'></div>忠懿王文武之才，于是乎亦可少窥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208817_comment'></div>靖康元年十一月二十二日，箕山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208817_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208818?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题鲁直尝新柑帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208818")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208818_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208818'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208818'>元祐末，有苏黄之称，渐不平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208818_comment'></div>或曰：「苏公自有芍药之评」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208818_comment'></div>恐未必然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208818_comment'></div>靖康元年十一月二十二日，箕山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1208818_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208820?labeling=true' "poem_title_1208820")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208820'>袁绍先笔，予近亦得试之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208820_comment'></div>《登真隐诀》在道藏中，公何必苦求耶？<div class='inline' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208819?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题鲁直章草颠草</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208819")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208819_comment'></div><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208819_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208819_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南门</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197453")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197453'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197453'>今上元年九月初，正南门锁涩关枢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197453'>城上日出三丈馀，城下戢戢人嗟吁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197453'>最怜纵横荷菜夫，欲杀青茜成蔫烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197453'>驴驼<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去。）</span>啮膝聚不驱，群鸡孤鹅鸣相呼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197453'>邈然不数半与猪，客子四散别门趋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197453'>逐臣过焉问何如，知者不告色不舒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197453'>或言上皇帝有符，北门不开留翠舆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197453'>金人忽屯城北隅，方今明日达聪俱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197453'>司门郎官上奏无，未几金人来坦涂。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197453'>城南铁骑柴<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去。）</span>奚车，焚荡辅郡陵别都。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197453'>衣冠南下满江湖，白头辞臣思献书。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197453'>洪范灾异信岂诬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_197453_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舟子语</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197391")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197391'>晁子被放逐，四方何所止。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197391'>随众到淮口，脱身乱兵里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197391'>长淮岁暮风，舟楫不得舣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197391'>因之狂雨来，青山白浪底。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197391'>风雨与波浪，三者酷斗靡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197391'>北客怖未尝，波神得自喜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197391'>舟子言勿怖，此是冲<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去。）</span>风尔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197391'>前风冲后风，纵神杂横鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197391'>吼怒夜潮落，倏忽熟<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作热）</span>风起。<div id='poem_sentence_8_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197391'>冲风如小人，熟<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作热）</span>风若君子。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197391'>明日复冲风，又非前之比。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197391'>舟子言可贺，此风即当死。<div id='poem_sentence_11_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_197391'>盛大不死者，从何睹神理。<div id='poem_sentence_12_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_197391'>京贯黼攸辈，万货他手委。<div id='poem_sentence_13_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_197391'>官知其然欤，几年干天纪。<div id='poem_sentence_14_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_197391'>神降与人言，化酒幻桃李。<div id='poem_sentence_15_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_197391'>上真怒中华，实锡羯胡祉。<div id='poem_sentence_16_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_197391'>破我诸州镇，胡阵风从指。<div id='poem_sentence_17_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_197391'>汉兵遂喜北，不走即降矣。<div id='poem_sentence_18_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_197391'>风伯不祐我，岂独在兹水。<div id='poem_sentence_19_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_197391'>舟子语可书，聊以视知已。<div id='poem_sentence_20_197391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_197391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_197391_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄城中亲旧<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197253")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197253_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_197253_0'>① 时在惠济安下罢三字宫词（四库本注作时在惠济宫）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197253'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197253'>苍皇逐客投兰若，傍晓衾寒喜且惊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197253'>隐隐似闻开静版，沈沈欲歇读经声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197253'>好将迟暮此间过，强欲论思何处行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197253'>城里有谁能念我，劳渠努力致升平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197253'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197253_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197264?labeling=true' "poem_title_197264")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197264'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197264'>王畿胡骑满，何地可逃生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197264'>尽室半徒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>步，有舟无水行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197264'>长淮能见阻，久雨自难晴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197264'>杂立官称在，低头愧国荣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197264'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197264'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_197264_0'>⑴ 原作涂，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197264_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_197127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初到高邮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197127")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197127'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197127'>避难苍黄处处过，扁舟不复怯风波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197127'>禹功淮海施偏少，汉业东南得最多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197127'>几日兵强令虏退，今年米贱奈予何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197127'>孙公乡里仍堪住，愁访山斋空薜萝<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：孙公萃老，高邮人。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197127'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197127_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>穷途</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197418")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197418'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197418'>穷途无达士，今日信途穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197418'>处处兵如市，行行马似龙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197418'>魂迷公主馆，梦断翠微宫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197418'>欲向江东去，风波更几重。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197418'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197418_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题破琴诗后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年1月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208825")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208825'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208825'>予有王晋卿淡碧绢画《房琯悟前生图》，写此诗于其后，甲午年遭火矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208825_comment'></div>靖康丁未正月十三日晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1208825_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题无水池新砚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年1月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208830")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208830'>若砚不欲受水，则墨亦不欲磨砚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208830_comment'></div>至于笔不欲点墨，纸不欲落笔，惟投县过白纸者即得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208830_comment'></div>雨暗窗昏，旅思大不佳，书以示德全，而病目又不能写字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208830_comment'></div>正月二十二日天台教僧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1208830_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题黄龙山僧送善澄上人诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208831")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208831'>三槐王氏以重望著于世，自晋公始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208831_comment'></div>善澄上人，实晋公六世孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208831_comment'></div>初有所感，而为僧受具戒，游禅林，远极江湖之胜，得黄龙道场而止焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208831_comment'></div>不敢自放于斯也，复北抵河朔，乞众僧之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208831_comment'></div>于是黄龙大德曰德逢、善清、如山、惠古、宗秀、直言、绍明、重政相与赋诗送行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208831_comment'></div>予避贼高邮，获观览，欣然益叹刘梦得善论僧家之诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208831_comment'></div>因定而得境，故翛然以清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208831_comment'></div>由慧而遣辞，故粹然以丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208831_comment'></div>今于黄龙诸公见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208831_comment'></div>虽然，梦得知其正而未知其助也久矣，有正必待夫有助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208831_comment'></div>释门诸公挹山川之英，而绝尘垢之外，其翛然粹然者，岂非学士大夫为之助欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208831_comment'></div>汤休之诗，实自于鲍明远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208831_comment'></div>灵一律师之诗既学潘、阮、江、谢，而又得李华、朱放、张继、皇甫冉、张南史以游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208831_comment'></div>皎然禅师实谢灵运之裔孙，其相从则颜鲁公、韦苏州、孟襄阳、李袁州、陆长源、皇甫曾、陆羽、张志和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208831_comment'></div>广宣则韩吏部、柳柳州、刘白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208831_comment'></div>近时秘演从欧阳公，参寥从东坡，亦已众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208831_comment'></div>黄龙诸公，予不知师友谓谁，而江南诗人黄鲁直则其人欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208831_comment'></div>言公之字画，绝类鲁直，盖可见也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208831_comment'></div>鲁直死已久，计今江南必复有一鲁直出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208831_comment'></div>澄上人归山中与诸公亟访之，为我谢曰：今日贤者不宜以山中为乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208831_comment'></div>靖康丁未春晁伯以。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1208831_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李太白草书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208832")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208832'>葛叔忱豪放不群，客为叔忱叹李太白无字画传于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208832_comment'></div>叔忱一日偶在僧舍，纵笔作字一轴，自名之曰李太白书，以戏一世之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208832_comment'></div>且与其僧约曰：「异日无语人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208832_comment'></div>每欲其僧信于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208832_comment'></div>其所谓得之丹徒僧舍者，乃书之丹徒僧舍也，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208832_comment'></div>不信者请以三事质之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208832_comment'></div>昔人有一书曰《古今能书人姓名》，自谓悉尽矣，恨不得闻见而录之也，乃独于白而遗之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208832_comment'></div>以故《法书要录》、《法书苑》、《墨薮》诸家，皆无白书之品第也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208832_comment'></div>白自负王霸之略，饮酒鼓琴，论兵击剑，鍊丹烧金，乘云仙去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208832_comment'></div>其志之所存者，靡不振发之，而草书奇屈如此，宁谦退自晦，无一字乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208832_comment'></div>白集有《怀素草书歌》，识者曰非白所作也，真伪未敢论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208832_comment'></div>要是白无一语自及其书，何邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208832_comment'></div>会稽湖上记者贺监与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208832_comment'></div>斯人清狂，捐落万事，顾肯孜孜收拾白藁草以欣戚耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208832_comment'></div>靖康丁未避地高邮任城，二十二叔父命书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1208832_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书与郭寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208833")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208833'>高邮郭四叔名寿，本名永寿，遇师得术，治疮疡痈疽，手出而愈，不以医自名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208833_comment'></div>常恨贱无以及物，幸此术以施所愿焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208833_comment'></div>特有所甚难者，不惜高价畜四方之真药，故其用药与人同，而功倍于人，未尝受人一钱以佐所费也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208833_comment'></div>仆去年冬，自睢阳避金贼至高邮，夏五月悲伤郁塞中，疽发于背，赖叔脱死而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208833_comment'></div>与叔语，盖类五戒道人，有得于中而忘于外者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208833_comment'></div>仆将何以谢之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208833_comment'></div>而叔知之，知所贵莫如文辞，欲吾之言以为好，于是乎书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1208833_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答张颐先辈书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208762")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208762'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208762'>说之启：衰暮留落高邮，首得尊公申两家五世之旧，足下不必以书为贽见过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208762_comment'></div>足下少年有辞章，不能自抑，有所怀，又思舒展，则其以书为贽见过，重可喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208762_comment'></div>足下所及甚高，顾兹血泪气绝之馀，莫知所以报者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208762_comment'></div>徘徊久之，辄奋然曰：披席之子，何妨门户之洿耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208762_comment'></div>顷年尝作《九学论》一篇，偶获存于金贼残毁故楮中，谨以为今日之献，惟望深考云尔，惟太史公每深考而得之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208762_comment'></div>悲哉学之难也，惟虞翻苦学，乃能叹嗟者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208762_comment'></div>老仆作《九学论》，虽尝见称于郑洛学者，而蒙东都之士诋诮亦不少，足下以谓如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208762_comment'></div>勉旃勉旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208762_comment'></div>五月十一日，说之上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1208762_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208989' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208989' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208989?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈键字子感序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208989")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208989_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208989'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208989'>陈延孺名其子曰键，是子思肖其名，来乞字于族舅晁伯以父曰：「君子自重则威，以毛发之身独立于四海九牧之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208989_comment'></div>及其务学也，徒步千里从师，洒扫应对，为作都养，不忌不惮，曰吾将无所不学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208989_comment'></div>太史公于晏子愿执鞭吾夫子之御，则未尝人其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208989_comment'></div>舅学《易》，知其所以然者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208989_comment'></div>予应之曰：心思不萌而为作不立，而名曰寂然不动，一身为天下之大键也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208989_comment'></div>无物以感我，而无物而不感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208989_comment'></div>宇宙豁如也，鬼神昭如也，前日之键，今日之通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208989_comment'></div>字汝曰子感，汝勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208989_comment'></div>建炎元年十有二月二十九日，真州江岸序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1208989_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197267?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_197267'>冰霜岁暮时，泽国更何为。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197267'>菰米经寒涩，芦门避乱宜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197201'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197201_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_196991_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197319?labeling=true' class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197319")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197319_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197319'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197319'>弟书毗陵来，有同股分刃之刀，绿管白毫之笔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197319'>刀是宝公锡上之所悬，笔亦江淹梦中之所得。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197319'>江南刀笔有如此，不比丰沛吏萧曹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>而兴锋镝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197319'>顾惟二物大有恨，不蒙独孤府君一言之饰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197319'>使君惠山延陆羽，文章不落翰墨迹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197319'>及今有用正劳劳，破贼露布征兵檄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197319'>小楷帖黄奏北阙，念弟未归空叹息。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_197319_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197319'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_197319_0'>⑴ 四库本作萧曹吏丰沛</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197319_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_197521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱德载以临江朱玠笔见赠以诗谢之德载与李先之亦相善</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197521'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197521'>清江长官空书来，朱玠妙笔空悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_197446'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197446'>双庙之前扁舟舣，太原失守胡尘起。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197446'>铁马渡河京城闭，堤上奔亡如磨蚁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197446'>不是清河早腹<span id='poem_sentence_3_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197446'>阉贯枭颅一日间，地下未应有馁鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197446'>董卓灯脐照傕汜，禄山肠流盛安使<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作史）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197446'><sup id='poem_sentence_8_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_197446'>尊名重器假狗彘，公卿何人是知理。<div id='poem_sentence_9_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_197446'>嗟予老病岂乐生，实抱忠谋难须死。<div id='poem_sentence_10_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_197446'>亦尝奏对明光殿，寒饥徒步荆棘里。<div id='poem_sentence_11_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_197446'>面风背日若有待，前有戎车后妻子。<div id='poem_sentence_12_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_197446'>戎车不断顿都城，元戎一言左右以。<div id='poem_sentence_13_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_197446'>遥有人家投宿无，骨肉夜饭无钝齿。<div id='poem_sentence_14_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_197446'>不嗟五日不颒面，但怜一夜灯花喜。<div id='poem_sentence_15_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_197446'>庶几明发脱盗手，复见皇威振遐迩。<div id='poem_sentence_16_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_197446'>庙堂再见谢太傅，奕棋未罢风尘弭。<div id='poem_sentence_17_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_197446'>前夜客投佛寺晚，全家冻泣木鱼底。<div id='poem_sentence_18_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_197446'>我今朝夕幸已多，闻见纷纷聊实纪。<div id='poem_sentence_19_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_197446'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_197446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197446'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_197446_0'>⑴ 自注：此二句谓贯虽枭，而用范讷辈。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_197446_0'>⑵ 自注：此二句谓京、黼辈党（原缺，据四库本补）与犹众。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197446_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_197449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枕上闻蛩忽久不鸣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197449")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197449'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197449'>促织复促织，尔实借我职<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作诲我力）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197449'>语我以诗书，觉我以道德。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197449'>胡然久不鸣，似知不如默。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197449'>默而如见容，实惟已失则。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197449'>不见容而疑，岂不云大惑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197449'>智或神于蓍，梦有不待卜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197449'>秋风日已高，太白光如植。<div id='poem_sentence_6_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_197449'>予岂默默时，杀身徇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>吾国。<div id='poem_sentence_7_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_197449'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_197449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197449'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_197449_0'>⑴ 原作循，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197449_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

泰州（海陵）
