id='poem_sentence_2_197225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197225'>日日凄风兼苦雨，要知寒食客愁真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197225'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197225_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太极传后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208781")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208781'>仆年二十有四，偶脱去科举事业，决意为五经之学，不专为一家章句也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208781_comment'></div>是时王氏之说列于学官者既尊，而又日有新说至自金陵，学者耻其得之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208781_comment'></div>从而士子又务为新异之说，寒士非其党者，莫能向迩以一言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208781_comment'></div>仆恨焉，岂无古人之师乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208781_comment'></div>果于《易》得孟喜、京房、郑康成、虞翻、关子明之徒，使小王之说不得一日容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208781_comment'></div>虽然，因是数家异乎王氏则有之，其于圣人制作之本意，又不知果否合否如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208781_comment'></div>逮绍圣戊寅邂逅洛阳，杨老朝散贤宝语及《易》而异之，良非仆平生所尝闻之之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208781_comment'></div>恳从杨老有求，乃得康节先生自为《易图》二，虽輹轮俱存，而杨行年将七十，中风，语音清浊不端，无由诘问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208781_comment'></div>二三年少在旁，难以其哂笑，仆独敬杨之老而尊其图，谓必可入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208781_comment'></div>杨且指《乾》、《坤》、《坎》、《离》四卦为仆言曰：「得是四卦，则见伏羲之《易》矣，而文王《易》在其中也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208781_comment'></div>越明日，如迷人识归路，有感于二图可指，循环无方体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208781_comment'></div>杨老曰：「吾昏病而忘之已久，今日因子之言，则如初授此图时也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208781_comment'></div>自是入洛与先生之子伯温游，得先生之遗编残稿，宝而藏之，服勤不知昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208781_comment'></div>二十年间，辄作《易传》四种，名曰《商瞿传》视其有师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208781_comment'></div>无何，靖康元年丙午冬，金贼猖狂至南京，所为《商瞿传》者与平生衣冠、五世图书悉以灰烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208781_comment'></div>既而避难高邮，从亲朋之请，追作《易传》数帙，未有条理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208781_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申正月，真州巨寇遽至，而高邮之传又复灰烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208781_comment'></div>是时老病之躯存于灰烬之外者幸也，乃避地海陵，病能饮食，而于《易》则曰不能，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208781_comment'></div>益为亲朋以追作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208781_comment'></div>起是年四月十八日辛未，讫七月一日癸未，凡用七十有二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208781_comment'></div>稿草具，或忘其旧，或得厥新，凡六卷，名之曰《太极传》，又有《外传》一卷，《因说》一卷，备为《易》一家之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208781_comment'></div>后有好古识变之君子，恐未必以仆言为妄作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208781_comment'></div>呜呼，吾道其亦艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208781_comment'></div>其亦艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208781_comment'></div>八月二十五日，海陵旅次，嵩阳景迂生晁说之记，年七十。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1208781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>三月上书宰相黄潜善申领差遣。作品：《与黄丞相书》<div id='poem_1208774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与黄丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208774")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208774'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208774'>说之惶恐死罪，再拜上启仆射相公黄阁之下：说之不度量，去月尝以流落羁旅仅存之身，饥饿将无粥以食，而狼狈于非舟非屋之居，控告下执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208774_comment'></div>如闻相公欲以江浙一支郡相处，不知其郡果如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208774_comment'></div>窃料相公必有以仁之，于是举家始有生人之色，以相属曰：「杀我者一时之否运也，生我者相公一言以倾否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208774_comment'></div>不然何以见于相公造命之功，不使一物失所之德，而建中兴伟绩者，岂不在是乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208774_comment'></div>然俟命于一之日而疑，多艰龃龉之人，未应有此响应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208774_comment'></div>二之日而惧，虽有牧养细民之微诚，而身无以自养也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208774_comment'></div>逮今三之日而不疑不惧者，羊叔之德难名，而王导之功不减管夷吾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208774_comment'></div>且复申之于相公，谢安能屈大司马而不能处王右军，本朝王文正公则从容以厚杨大年，大年分司在阳翟而求颍，不失为汝海守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208774_comment'></div>相公方为明时修祖宗故事，独容文正公优于文靖乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208774_comment'></div>相公岂不闻函牛之鼎乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208774_comment'></div>函牛之鼎最难为功，蔡邕能以言边让而闻之于何进，则是鼎也，终难以自言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208774_comment'></div>惟相公始终之仁，有不待区区之言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208774_comment'></div>薄遽不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208774_comment'></div>四月二日，说之再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1208774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在海陵。作品：《题刘器之与陈止之书》《题宋宣献帖》《题陆子履帖》《跋无咎兄所作李季良字叙》《威德军节度使嘉国公诗集序》《题李公择尚书宣谕》《题石曼卿送周卿游边》《跋沈睿达写桃源图》《题张泰然清白堂记》《流寓海陵半年……》《周与可子景夏序》《题僧希白摹法帖》《题晋上人智果帖》《题周景夏所藏东坡帖》《跋赵清献帖与故人周尉子六秀才帖》<div id='poem_1208837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题宋宣献帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208837")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208837'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208837'>常山公有书名一时，蔡君不能掩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208837_comment'></div>兹二帖益重吾两家事契哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208837_comment'></div>建炎戊申上巳，海陵旅舍晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208837_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题陆子履帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208838")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208838'>陆子履少有书名，而晚年名似减，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208838_comment'></div>惟欧阳公始终眷眷于斯人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208838_comment'></div>建炎戊申上巳，拥火海陵旅舍中，晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208838_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋无咎兄所作李季良字叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208839")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208839'>说之获观季良父诗后数日，观此序，重增叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208839_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申三月九日海陵旅次。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1208839_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>威德军节度使嘉国公诗集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208790")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208790'>窃以艺祖受天丕命，臣妾万方，干戈不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208790_comment'></div>太宗、仁宗尚文崇儒，不待浸昌，荡然百年鲸鲵，一日悉仪孔鸾，天下纯归王道，大夫学士耻言财利而识廉耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208790_comment'></div>矧在宗室子孙，冠婚车服饮食，纤悉毕仰县官，殆不知其货利于我何为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208790_comment'></div>礼义积而文章出矣，盖不知有一经之士而备五经名目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208790_comment'></div>《尚书》始或尽瘁于所难，而远究科斗古文篆籀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208790_comment'></div>从上之好而学虞永兴书，往往逼金石，其飞白则众且尽善矣，是岂出于他哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208790_comment'></div>不强以法度，不冒以官职，人得日竭其聪明，优游于所好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208790_comment'></div>上以岁时锡宴广内，用家人礼，笑语尽醉，即席赋诗，罚其未成者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208790_comment'></div>于时法度莫我阻，而亦弗官之，吾荣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208790_comment'></div>不知何事，此风顿息，宗子翘然陋昔之人，其言则高矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208790_comment'></div>有能不外慕、不近名，兀兀若终身无恨者，其惟故通州防御使、赠威德军节度使、追封嘉国公令畯乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208790_comment'></div>景升为人孝友恭敬，无他好，而唯学之嗜，忘寒暑昼夜疾病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208790_comment'></div>居有高楼，程课不下，手抄卷轴，戢戢笋束，不知几十百之多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208790_comment'></div>每见而叹之曰：「少年举子而发愤，白首腐儒欲罢而不能，其在王孙何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208790_comment'></div>抑可以观祖宗之遗泽乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208790_comment'></div>间取古今法书图画自娱乐，曰：「彼之所得，亦吾所能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208790_comment'></div>吾志之鼓吹，有诗存焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208790_comment'></div>吾诗之丹青，有画存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208790_comment'></div>以故其诗闲而有风，不勤意而趣远，若愿而无所求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208790_comment'></div>余每谓前不亲炙于梅圣俞，后不曲从于黄鲁直，他人未易景升之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208790_comment'></div>予交于景升父子间，自予抱病逃难，远旅海陵，因其丹青而益爱其诗，不鼓以吹，而忘吾干戈垂死之厄，爽然自位于升平之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208790_comment'></div>子子笈请予题于编首，其可辞之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208790_comment'></div>建炎二年三月二十三日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1208790_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题李公择尚书宣谕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208842")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208842'>卿博通史学，入侍金华，多所发明，深副虚宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208842_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1208842'>祖宗时，讲筵尚耆艾，相与尊先儒，不过明训诂，有听而无难，不足于言而有馀于行，进退容止肃如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208842_comment'></div>当宁望之，宁待其言之华哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208842_comment'></div>近时务以英俊为讲席之宠，悉反旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208842_comment'></div>如元祐中李尚书之口宣，当上之史官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208842_comment'></div>建炎二年三月壬寅，海陵旅次晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1208842_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题石曼卿送周卿游边</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208840")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208840'>观曼卿书，想见其谈兵，虽范文正公不能折也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208840_comment'></div>要在尹师鲁顿挫耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208840_comment'></div>清明后一日，箕山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208840_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋沈睿达写桃园图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208841")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208841'>治平、熙宁间，睿达书名，自浙江振京师，谁知有东坡书哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208841_comment'></div>况又十五馀年后，称黄鲁直书，至于内人裙带事，识者犹为睿达叹息之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208841_comment'></div>建炎戊申清明后一日，箕山晁伯以父。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208841_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题张泰然清白堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208843")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208843'>唐陈子昂、吕温皆自铭其世德云：「取法于古人，而世人无知吾家之所积者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208843_comment'></div>泰然于《清白记》何嫌！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208843_comment'></div>建炎戊申四月癸亥，嵩山晁说之题海陵旅舍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208843_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>流寓海陵半年忽得周元仲分宁书欣慰与常日不同辄有作代书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197513")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_197513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197513'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197513'>海陵士子江东客，我到海陵无主人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197513'>苍波知君到何处，直待书来消息真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197513'>与君相去岁月久，世事茫茫谁出手。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197513'>桑田欲变仙人去，鹤驾云轩安得取。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197513'>愁肠出泪付沧波，江上秋风奈我何。<div id='poem_sentence_4_197513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_197513'>何处云山君待我，更烦先寄䌽云歌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_197513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_197513'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_197513_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周与可字景夏序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208990")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208990'>海陵周与可字从之，问嵩山晁说之求易其字，曰：「我于兹未安也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208990_comment'></div>曰：子未安子夏之论交乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208990_comment'></div>噫子夏之论交，当时见隘于子张，今日为东坡先生玉石之，亦不幸欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208990_comment'></div>谨稽诸夫子「主忠信，无友不如己」之言，而得师于三人行之中，好恶惟乡人之道义而是非之，则其与可而拒不可者，非子夏之言也，实本诸夫子之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208990_comment'></div>盖言有近乎尤而卒无所戾者，子夏之言是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208990_comment'></div>言有听之若可喜，而究之亦无以异乎前人者，子张之言是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208990_comment'></div>尊贤而容众，嘉善而矜不能，贤则于人无不容，不贤则不足以自容一己，亦徒异乎子夏云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208990_comment'></div>若是时，子夏与子张面辩以一言，则千载好憎，门阑不分矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208990_comment'></div>东坡先生于子夏取其与不取其拒，惟子张之是，不知不能者受我之矜焉，则内愧而去者不少矣，其拒斯人也亦不浅矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208990_comment'></div>敢字子曰景夏，复古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208990_comment'></div>《易·同人》初九「同人于门无咎」，子夏以之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208990_comment'></div>上九「同人于郊无悔」，子张以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208990_comment'></div>《大有》九四「匪其彭，无咎」，子夏以之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208990_comment'></div>九二「大车以载，有攸往，无咎」，子张以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208990_comment'></div>其所以安身崇德而无咎者，实不甚相远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208990_comment'></div>其在后世而敝，则子张者公孙弘也，子夏则汲黯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208990_comment'></div>子纯明而自信，不妄与人交，必知所择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208990_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申七月十七日旅舍序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1208990_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题僧希白摹法帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208844")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208844'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208844'>僧希白书，豪放自得，恨平生功浅，乃手摹内法帖，而不能没其俊气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208844_comment'></div>东坡故不喜王著之拘，而喜白之逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208844_comment'></div>戊申七月二十七日，海陵旅舍伯以父。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208844_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋赵清献帖与故人周尉之子六秀才帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208850")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208850'>清献公之帖，岂独为周氏之荣于时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208850_comment'></div>邦家、朋友、故旧、风俗之美，公之力顾弗多邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208850_comment'></div>建炎戊申八月一日，嵩山晁说之海陵旅舍题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208850_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1208850_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在海陵长达半年余。作品：《题赵清献与周彭泽诗》《题写本老子后》《汝南主客文集序》《宋故平恩府晁公墓表》《新年》《感事》《海陵闲居》《三岁》《闻富季申迁校书郎》《自适》<div id='poem_1208851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题赵清献与周彭泽诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208851")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208851'>此诗其传则清献公所作，彭泽君之志非略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208851_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申八月一日，海陵旅次嵩山晁说之题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208851_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1208851_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题写本老子后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208803")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208803'>此书故题曰《老子道德经》，胜于分道德为两经者，其文字稍近古，特录之，自便观览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208803_comment'></div>窃惟伏羲、文王、周公赞《易》之后，惟老氏得《易》之变通屈伸，知柔而贵虚，务应而不得，殷勤以立言，幸乎此书之存也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208803_comment'></div>逮夫孔子系《易》之后，此书则为一偏之言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208803_comment'></div>责贤者备也，世犹有《老》、《易》之称，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208803_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申八月五日，海陵旅舍嵩山晁说之题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1208803_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汝南主客文集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1208791")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208791'>士有有其实而名不与之俱，或得名一切而违其实，方以耻我，乃欲以我荣诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208791_comment'></div>此人君当宁日以求士，而左右大臣蔽之之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208791_comment'></div>或有千百而一，自达于人主前者，不蔽之，则忌之，幸得逃罪谴者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208791_comment'></div>无曰此细事也，实世之治乱兴亡系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208791_comment'></div>说之从世父新知蔡州、故尚书主客郎中，生知所学，少有辞赋声名出诸生上，其仕既久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208791_comment'></div>大臣方平居无心于除吏时，每见公，曰：「诏刊七史，公也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208791_comment'></div>且复叹曰：「『礼乐终梁绝，文章过魏残』，真是绝唱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208791_comment'></div>是公礼部优等奏名时所赋诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208791_comment'></div>公释褐以甲科为常州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208791_comment'></div>时知州事陈公襄，四先生之一也，肇兴学校，躬横经为诸生以讲，勤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208791_comment'></div>而王平甫以布衣专主说书，有霍汉英、李公弼者豪英，不特为东南之秀也，且以头角诸生数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208791_comment'></div>公有职事在学校，诸生从公，有闻见，服膺无异辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208791_comment'></div>嗟夫，公少仕以文学著也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208791_comment'></div>逮公三年免丧之后，始有新学，而先王之经亦以新名之，公自伤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208791_comment'></div>乃为青州寿光县主簿，或不以簿书勾考待公者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208791_comment'></div>时清献赵公帅青，公独叹曰：「吾不得于薄而得于厚矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208791_comment'></div>清献公初入境时，荐公为州教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208791_comment'></div>时相滋不喜曰：「赵阅道以谓文学士也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208791_comment'></div>公自兹久于粗官而甘心焉，亦绝口不为人道简编中一字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208791_comment'></div>居无几何，上念高丽表章美可观，诏掌高丽书状者慎其选，无自屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208791_comment'></div>宰相谓公乃可奉诏，于是公复以文学称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208791_comment'></div>或谓公是行也，有母老可辞，而公白相府曰：「幸与高丽国王并通闺籍，顾书状官礼数如何，非不荣，斯赏格懋也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208791_comment'></div>盖前未有以朝臣职是行焉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208791_comment'></div>公乃复与刀笔吏游，而钱谷得意少年，谓公易与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208791_comment'></div>公出有使节郡符，入而闲居挂冠，默以文章事付诸后进，意若讳其少时所能者，茫然自不省平生藁草尝有无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208791_comment'></div>公季子谦之年十有三岁，窃有志焉，如人适嗜好而勤收拾，无远迩，唯恐公一字留落也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208791_comment'></div>乃得公诗若干，杂文、论、表章若干，定著为若干卷，以待后之览者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208791_comment'></div>泰山或有不见者，而岩为万国之尊则自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208791_comment'></div>东坡为兵部尚书，公丞太仆，以事谒省部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208791_comment'></div>时天寒甚，东坡命酒手以觞公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208791_comment'></div>公色动，若不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208791_comment'></div>东坡叹曰：「何姬公三十年时，今乐府辞盛于诸公间，窃与游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208791_comment'></div>孰谓公嗟咤至是乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208791_comment'></div>公与豫章黄鲁直周旋而唱和多矣，齐鲁彼此者，果孰为笃论也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208791_comment'></div>公于一世交游真得泛焉而亲焉者，以有德归范彝叟，而心向之馀则宁轻富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208791_comment'></div>而不忌语言，以轩轾一坐，若无人焉者，难谓公以他人并范也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208791_comment'></div>公之不愧屋漏则然矣，而于屋漏有愧者，果足以知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208791_comment'></div>惟知公于士，泾渭源委湛如，不可荡漾，然后知公之文先灌后索云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208791_comment'></div>谦之与说之同避地海陵，偶兵火未服两骖时，难忘五世承平图书之好，乃请说之序公见存之集，何以辞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208791_comment'></div>公讳端仁，字尧民，末得知蔡州，未果行，以疾卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208791_comment'></div>谨题其集曰《汝南主客集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208791_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申九月十六日，从侄具官说之谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1208791_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1209035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1209035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1209035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故平恩府君晁公墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎二年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_1209035")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1209035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1209035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1209035'>晁氏东眷舒州郎中元配公孙氏第三子，其字次膺，生而俊气干云霄直上，与先生长者语，无难事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1209035_comment'></div>识与不识见之，曰：「是诸公卿之选已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1209035_comment'></div>学辞赋于诸兄间，日一再作而佳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1209035_comment'></div>京师秋赋，而时方以理财为新政，主文刘贡父、李公择、王忠甫皆与丞相论不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1209035_comment'></div>试《节以制度不伤财赋》，公选甚高，礼部不奏名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1209035_comment'></div>既而废诗赋，用新经义，公曰：「人各有才智而喜异也，是不待一再作者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1209035_comment'></div>主王氏《诗》，犹杂以毛公《诗》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1209035_comment'></div>登熙宁六年进士科，注单州城武县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1209035_comment'></div>时初遣察访使出按郡国不法，远迩震恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1209035_comment'></div>使京东者少年新进，未更仕任，特恃其兄参知政事与丞相方睦劾一路，有几人可免不坐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1209035_comment'></div>是人方仰公气象，而不得不听其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1209035_comment'></div>于是京东有宽政，莫知其自公出，而人被赐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1209035_comment'></div>以瀛州防御推官知洺州平恩县，县滨河，公与众游乐，而独色忧曰：「河不决今年则明年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1209035_comment'></div>乃舒以调度，民知无征，而不知有储也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1209035_comment'></div>后有小吴之役，一道远迩病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1209035_comment'></div>而平恩之民因以叹公神明之政，德之，今不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1209035_comment'></div>代还，格碍，不得改官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1209035_comment'></div>以泰宁军节度推官知大名府莘县事，民相庆曰：「平恩之父母也，肯独不以吾属为莘人之子乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1209035_comment'></div>公于莘得上下之欣喜，而誉益远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1209035_comment'></div>在平恩时，上位居官如故，而待公犹故旧朋友也，置不举属吏礼数，而转运使李楚老犹不平，阴以怒提举保甲狄咨，按刺公以保甲法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1209035_comment'></div>时保甲之法密秋荼也，孰非保甲法之罪人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1209035_comment'></div>前日以公为才而肃给异功状者，为今私不奉法，而于时政有向背矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1209035_comment'></div>狱具，除仕籍，居楚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1209035_comment'></div>大赦，居兖州，渐以还济州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1209035_comment'></div>公裕然不以欣戚于去来，曰：「舌不在，不得自致其身也邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1209035_comment'></div>公初于济贫甚，何心于吾富哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1209035_comment'></div>人术甚疏，而殆天有以富之也，乃知天命祐之而行者君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1209035_comment'></div>公于是居闲将十年，犹一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1209035_comment'></div>视一世之进退穷达，须臾歌笑，蹙蹙涂上多平生故人，曰：「孰能为我往谢之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1209035_comment'></div>嗟夫，公能贫而富，穷以达，使用其才于朝，宜何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1209035_comment'></div>元祐初有理诉所，公亦未忍自弃于兹时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1209035_comment'></div>彼在位者乃不得特恩洗涤公，必欲以散官论如常法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1209035_comment'></div>公去弗顾曰：「知命乃为君子邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1209035_comment'></div>议者谓元丰多失士，而元祐之失士亦不少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1209035_comment'></div>其在公，特不仁者，顾岂不有一哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1209035_comment'></div>一林之木异质，先伐之材，风雨既先摧之，孰肯出力以培之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1209035_comment'></div>此君子之困幽谷，所以不觌三年也，或终身幽谷而与株木处矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1209035_comment'></div>虽然，使公之官于朝也，亦几何时留哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1209035_comment'></div>识者谓使朝廷之弃公，不若公初自郡国弃之也，闻者悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1209035_comment'></div>公闲居何以发挥其伊郁侘傺之感哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1209035_comment'></div>自念《离骚》之变《国风》，宋玉、景差之徒殆不知有《国风》者，非忘之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1209035_comment'></div>其后以宫商为乐府者，又自一《离骚》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1209035_comment'></div>以故公于是辞有律吕矣，其传寖远，上达于六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1209035_comment'></div>会新作大晟府，起黄钟于上躬之中，指弃塞古今诸儒异同之论，坐取三代以来钟鼎磬镈镛铣之属毁而碎之，视不复用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1209035_comment'></div>昭陵留心，躬以封缄之品，度亦不可存矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1209035_comment'></div>师臣末为此媚上之术，鼓舞天下，要得天下咸知其不可起而仕者，必为我出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1209035_comment'></div>公乃被迅召入大晟府，奉旨作为一时瑞物之辞，乃还公承事郎、大晟府按协声律，咸曰彻乎其众望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1209035_comment'></div>盖公于语言酬酢之初，失师臣之微矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1209035_comment'></div>是行也，不知公者谓公喜矣，知公者为公耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1209035_comment'></div>呜呼，前谓公仕于朝而达也，亦能久而待其才之输乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1209035_comment'></div>彼李固、杜乔辈于汉祚三绝，人君残昏失道之时，能为其次而不能为其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1209035_comment'></div>五王黜周后，反唐帝，歛天下之情，而一日身之敏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1209035_comment'></div>然能勇决于临事，而迟疑于来事，二者相望于千岁，而不保其躬，卒贻后世纷纭之大患则一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1209035_comment'></div>公有以当斯任也，必见功烈之出非常，而不终日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1209035_comment'></div>其他脂韦之厚薄，尚敢为公陈哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1209035_comment'></div>有以乐府辞为公称者，重可悲乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1209035_comment'></div>公政和三年七月二十三日以疾卒于昭德外第，实至京之踰月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1209035_comment'></div>娶梁氏，男三人：益之、观之、同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1209035_comment'></div>女三人，婿曰滕伯奇、翟光弼、马承休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1209035_comment'></div>以其年九月十九日葬鱼山世墓之次，后十有三年说之避地海陵，乃得论次表公之墓如上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1209035_comment'></div>建炎二年戊申九月甲申，从侄具官说之撰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1209035_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_196982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/196982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新年</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_196982")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_196982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_196982'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_196982'>何事重新作此年，身无疾病意欣然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_196982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_196982'>春风莫但开桃李，吹落妖星静九天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196982'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196982_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197224' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197224' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197224?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海陵閒居</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197224")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197224_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197224'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197224'>春色海边虽到晚，幽居亦且得徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197224'>风轻花影閒閒去，人静<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作院静）</span>棋声揭揭来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197224'>莫话艰难催白发，从教颠倒长青苔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197224'>明朝此兴如能在，梦到梁王旧吹台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197224'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197224_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三岁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197333")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197333'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197333'>羁离已三岁，几处幸容身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197333'>有梦延秋雨，无言问虏尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197333'>伤今多难日，忆我太平人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197333'>雨露随行在，公卿几番新。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197333'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197333_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻富季申迁校书郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197210")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197210'>小富秋来慰所望，青衫叙进校书郎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197210'>相公勋业久弥著，孙子门阑渐有光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197210'>莫话诗过已埋没，且非碗脱得分张。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197210'>白莲逋客独惆怅，泪尽西风归政堂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197210'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_197210'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_197210_0'>⑴ 自注：卷里诗过一千首，白头来作校书郎，谓王建云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_197210_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_197117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自适</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197117")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197117'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197117'>避难三年百感生，众虽溷浊自澄清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197117'>閒窥鸟雀往来势，静听儿童读诵声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197117'>但道孤生元废弃，莫言频数论平生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197117'>大河今岁如为用，即看千官赴上京。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197117'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197117_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　冬，渡江寓金陵。作品：《月下渡金陵江》<div id='poem_196737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_196737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_196737'>只今江月交光夜，情似月明愁似江。<div id='poem_sentence_1_196737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_196737'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_196737_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　在金陵。作品：《金陵二首》<div id='poem_197177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197177?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金陵二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27342, "宋", "晁说之", "poem_title_197177")'>晁说之</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197177'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197177'>金陵形势眼中见，一吊兴亡梦寐间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197177'>侯景长驱走龙虎，王敦内叛压江山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197177'>中原有主申明命，下国何人敢肆奸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197177'>白首自伤归未得，此身何处得清閒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197177_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_197177'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_197177_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_197176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_197176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/197176?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_197176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_197176'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_197176'>上帝于人靡有常，江流何处任兴亡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_197176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_197176'>干戈揖逊一锡杖，社稷山川半面妆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_197176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_197176'>故自无人比叔子，尚怜有意保襄阳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_197176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_197176'>白头难待太平策，万国明朝建治康。<div id='poem_sentence_3_197176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　正月七日卒，赠通奉大夫。<br /></div>
